# Gwen DSL

:::tip
Use the DSL to compose [StepDefs](/docs/meta#stepdefs) in your [meta](/docs/meta).
:::

## DSL Reference

All Gherkin steps that match the DSL expressions described here are readily executable by Gwen. The DSL matched is the operation that will be performed at execution time.

### Bindings

#### Text bindings

<details id="name-is-value">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is "<value>"
  ```
  <p>Binds the given value to a name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;value&gt;</code> is the value to bind (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    Given my name is "Gwen"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-value">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-literal">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is <blank|empty|true|false>
  ```
  <p>Binds a literal value to a name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the literal value to</li>
    
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    Given my name is blank
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-literal">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.59.0">v3.59.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### File bindings

<details id="name-is-defined-by-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by file "<filepath>"
  ```
  <p>Associates a name with the contents of a file. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to associated the file contents</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code> or <code>@Lazy</code></Link> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either annotation, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    Given the content is defined by file "path/to/file.txt"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.11.0">v1.11.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-encoding-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by <encoding> file "<filepath>"
  ```
  <p>Associates a name with the contents of a file using a given character encoding. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to associated the file contents</li>
    <li><code>&lt;encoding&gt;</code> is the <Link to="https://docs.oracle.com/javase/8/docs/technotes/guides/intl/encoding.doc.html">encoding</Link> to use when reading the file</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code> or <code>@Lazy</code></Link> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either annotation, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    Given the content is defined by UTF-8 file "path/to/file.txt"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-encoding-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.71.0">v3.71.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Regex bindings

<details id="name-is-defined-in-text-ref-by-regex-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined in <textRef> by regex "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Captures text from a text reference using the given regex expression and associates it with the given name. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the name to associate the captured value to</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the regex selector expression</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code>, <code>@Lazy</code></Link> or <code>@Masked</code> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either of the above annotations, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
      <li><code>@Masked</code> masks the captured value to prevent it from being logged as clear text</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the date is "2021-09-22"
      And the year is defined in the date by regex "(\d{4})"
     Then the year should be "2021"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-in-text-ref-by-regex-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### XML bindings

<details id="name-is-defined-by-the-node-type-in-xml-ref-by-xpath-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by the <nodeType> in <xmlRef> by xpath "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Captures content from a referenced XML value using the given XPath expression and associates it with the given name. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the name to associate the captured value to</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;nodeType&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to capture the text node</li>
        <li><code>node</code> to capture a single node</li>
        <li><code>nodeset</code> to capture multiple nodes</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;xmlRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the XML source
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to XML text, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code>, <code>@Lazy</code></Link> or <code>@Masked</code> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either of the above annotations, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
      <li><code>@Masked</code> masks the captured value to prevent it from being logged as clear text</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the xml is "<result><status>passed</status></result>"
      And status is defined by the text in the xml by xpath "//result/status"
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-the-node-type-in-xml-ref-by-xpath-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### JSON bindings

<details id="name-is-defined-in-json-ref-by-json-path-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined in <jsonRef> by json path "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Captures content from a referenced JSON value using the given JSON path expression and associates it with the given name. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the name to associate the captured value to</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;nodeType&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to capture the text node</li>
        <li><code>node</code> to capture a single node</li>
        <li><code>nodeset</code> to capture multiple nodes</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;sourceRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the XML source
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to XML text, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code>, <code>@Lazy</code></Link> or <code>@Masked</code> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either of the above annotations, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
      <li><code>@Masked</code> masks the captured value to prevent it from being logged as clear text</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the json is "{ "status": "passed" }"
      And the status is defined in the json by json path "$.status"
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-in-json-ref-by-json-path-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-content-in-element-by-json-path-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the content in <element> by json path "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures JSON content from a web element using the given JSON Path expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element containing the JSON content</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON selector</Link> expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # assuming a web element contains json: { "status": "passed" }
    Given the json web element can be located by id "json"
     When I capture the content in the json web element by json path "$.status" as the status
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-content-in-element-by-json-path-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### JS bindings

<details id="name-is-defined-by-javascript-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by <javascript|js> "<script>"
  ```
  <p>Associates a name with the return value of a JavaScript expression or function.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to associate</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript|js&gt;</code> is <code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>)</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;script&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or function that will return the value (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <ul>
          <li>For a one liner expression, no function, arrow declaration or <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
          <li>
            For a function, use either:
            <ul>
              <li><Link to="/docs/js-functions">Arrow syntax</Link> (preferred): <code>(arg1, arg2, ..argN) =&gt; &#123; body &#125;</code> (Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.56.0">v3.56.0</Link>)</li>
              <li>Or anonymous function syntax (legacy): <code>(function(arg1, arg2, ..argN)&#123; body &#125;)(arguments[0], arguments[1], ..arguments[N])</code></li>
            </ul>
          </li>
        </ul>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code>, <code>@Lazy</code></Link> or <code>@Masked</code> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either of the above annotations, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
      <li><code>@Masked</code> masks the captured value to prevent it from being logged as clear text</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given iso date is defined by js "new Date().toISOString().substring(0, 10)"
     Then iso date should match regex "^\d{4}-([0]\d|1[0-2])-([0-2]\d|3[01])$"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-javascript-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-js-function-applied-to-arg">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by <javascriptRef> applied to "<argument>"
  ```
  <p>Applies a JavaScript function to an argument and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the function result to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascriptRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the javascript function to apply</li>
    <li><code>&lt;argument&gt;</code> argument to apply the function</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code>, <code>@Lazy</code></Link> or <code>@Masked</code> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either of the above annotations, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
      <li><code>@Masked</code> masks the captured value to prevent it from being logged as clear text</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {9}
    Given iso date is defined by js "new Date().toISOString().substring(0, 10)"
      And toDMY is defined by js
          """
          (ymd) => {
            var parts = ymd.split('-');
            return parts[2] + '/' + parts[1] + '/' + parts[0];
          }
          """
      And dmy date is defined by toDMY applied to "${iso date}"
     Then dmy date should match regex "^([0-2]\d|3[01])/([0]\d|1[0-2])/\d{4}$"
  ```

  ```gherkin {9}
    Given toMDY is defined by js
          """
          (ymd) => {
            var months = ['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun', 'Jul', 'Aug', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec'];
            var parts = ymd.split('-');
            return months[parseInt(parts[1]) - 1] + ' ' + parts[2] + ' ' + parts[0];
          }
          """
      And dmy date is defined by toMDY applied to "2022-04-05"
     Then dmy date should be "Apr 05 2022"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-js-function-applied-to-arg">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.10.1">v3.10.1</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-js-function-applied-to-args-delimited-by">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by <javascriptRef> applied to "<arguments>" delimited by "<delimiter>"
  ```
  <p>Applies a JavaScript function to mutiple arguments using a customer delimiter and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the function result to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascriptRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the javascript function to apply</li>
    <li><code>&lt;arguments&gt;</code> a delimited list of arguments to apply the function to</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;delimiter&gt;</code> is the delmiter used in <code>&lt;arguments&gt;</code>
      <ul>
        <li>The 1st agrument is referenced in the JavaScript as <code>arguments[0]</code>, the 2nd argument as <code>arguments[1]</code>, the 3rd as <code>arguments[2]</code> and so on.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code>, <code>@Lazy</code></Link> or <code>@Masked</code> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either of the above annotations, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
      <li><code>@Masked</code> masks the captured value to prevent it from being logged as clear text</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given iso date is defined by js "new Date().toISOString().substring(0, 10)"
      And toDMY is defined by js "(y,m,d) => d + '/' + m + '/' + y"
      And dmy date is defined by toDMY applied to "${iso date}" delimited by "-"
     Then dmy date should match regex "^([0-2]\d|3[01])/([0]\d|1[0-2])/\d{4}$"
  ```
  
  ```gherkin {10}
    Given toISO is defined by js
          """
          (m,d,y) => {
            var months = ['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun', 'Jul', 'Aug', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec'];
            var mNo = months.indexOf(m) + 1;
            if (mNo < 10) mNo = '0' + mNo;
            return y + '-' + mNo + '-' + d;
          }
          """
      And iso date is defined by toISO applied to "Apr 05 2022" delimited by " "
     Then iso date should be "2022-04-05"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-js-function-applied-to-args-delimited-by">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.10.0">v3.10.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-js-function-applied-to-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by <javascriptRef> applied to <element>
  ```
  <p>Applies a JavaScript function to an element and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the function result to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascriptRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the javascript single argument function to apply</li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the web element to apply the function to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code>, <code>@Lazy</code></Link> or <code>@Masked</code> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately applies the function to the element and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> applies the function to the element and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either of the above annotations, the function is applied to the element every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
      <li><code>@Masked</code> masks the captured value to prevent it from being logged as clear text</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given getHref is defined by js "(elem) => elem.getAttribute('href')"
      And the todo link can be located by xpath "//a[contains(text(),'TodoMVC')]"
      And href is defined by getHref applied to the todo link
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist/"
     Then href should be "http://todomvc.com"
  ```
  
  ```gherkin {9}
    Given getHref is defined by js 
      """
      (elem) => { 
        return elem.getAttribute('href')
      }
      """
      And the todo link can be located by xpath "//a[contains(text(),'TodoMVC')]"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist/"
      And @Eager href is defined by getHref applied to the todo link
     Then href should be "http://todomvc.com"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-js-function-applied-to-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.6.0">v4.6.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### System Processes bindings

<details id="name-is-defined-by-system-process-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by system process "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Associates a name with the return value of a local system process. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to associated the returned value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the system process that will return the value to assign (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code>, <code>@Lazy</code></Link> or <code>@Masked</code> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either of the above annotations, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
      <li><code>@Masked</code> masks the captured value to prevent it from being logged as clear text</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given my hostname is defined by system process "hostname"
     Then my hostname should not be ""
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-system-process-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-system-process-expression-delimited-by-delimiters">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by system process "<expression>" delimited by "<delimiters>"
  ```
  <p>Associates a name with the return value of a delimited local system process. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to associated the returned value to</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the system process that will return the value to assign (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>Delmiters are required for special cases such as when unbalanced quoted strings are passed as arguments (see example).</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;delmiters&gt;</code> is a regex pattern defining the delimiter(s) used in <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code>, <code>@Lazy</code></Link> or <code>@Masked</code> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either of the above annotations, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
      <li><code>@Masked</code> masks the captured value to prevent it from being logged as clear text</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given my message is defined by system process "echo,"quoted text " and orphan quote"" delimited by ","
     Then my message should be ""quoted text " and orphan quote""
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-system-process-expression-delimited-by-delimiters">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-unix-system-process-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by unix system process "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Associates a name with the return value of a local unix system process. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to associated the returned value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the unix system process that will return the value to assign (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code>, <code>@Lazy</code></Link> or <code>@Masked</code> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either of the above annotations, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
      <li><code>@Masked</code> masks the captured value to prevent it from being logged as clear text</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  Given a <i>file.csv</i> with content:
  ```
  Word1,Word2,Compound
  basket,ball,basketball
  sun,flower,sunflower
  ```

  The following will print the data and line up each column

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given my table is defined by unix system process "cat file.csv | column -t -s\,"
     Then my table should be 
          """
          Word1   Word2   Compound
          basket  ball    basketball
          sun     flower  sunflower
          """
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-unix-system-process-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.19.0">v3.19.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Element locators

:::info Shadow DOM also supported
Since [v4.8.0](https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.8.0), you can use the `@ShadowRoot` annotation on any locator step to refer to a shadow root element.
<Link href="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/blob/master/src/test/features/shadowdom/ShadowDOM.feature">Example</Link>
:::

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>"
  ```

  <p>Binds a selector for a web element to the current scope with a default lookup timeout that can be overridden with the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
  ```

  With explicit timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given @Timeout('10s') the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
  ```

  Without any timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given @Timeout('0s') the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-at-index">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" at index <index>
  ```

  <p>Binds an indexed selector for a web element to the current scope with a default lookup timeout that can be overridden with the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;index&gt;</code> is the index of the element to select in list returned by <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given the first item can be located by css ".todo-list label" at index 0
     Then the first item should contain "Walk the dog"
  ```

  With explicit timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given @Timeout('12s') the first item can be located by css ".todo-list label" at index 0
     Then the first item should contain "Walk the dog"
  ```

  Without any timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given @Timeout('0s') the first item can be located by css ".todo-list label" at index 0
     Then the first item should contain "Walk the dog"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-at-index">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.28.0">v2.28.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-in-other-element-at-index">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" at index <index> in <otherElement>
  ```

  <p>Binds an indexed selector for a web element (contained in another) to the current scope with a default lookup timeout that can be overridden with the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;index&gt;</code> is the index of the element to select in list returned by <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code> is the name of the web element that this one is relative to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the count info can be located by class "todo-count"
      And the count unit can be located by tag "span" at index 1 in the count info
     Then the count unit should contain "item"
  ```

  With explicit timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given @Timeout('20s') the count info can be located by class "todo-count"
      And @Timeout('10s') the count unit can be located by tag "span" at index 1 in the count info
     Then the count unit should contain "item"
  ```

  Without any timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given @Timeout('0s') the count info can be located by class "todo-count"
      And @Timeout('0s') the count unit can be located by tag "span" at index 1 in the count info
     Then the count unit should contain "item"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-in-other-element-at-index">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.28.0">v2.28.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-with-fallbacks">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by
    | selector     | expression     |
    | <selector 1> | <expression 1> |
    | <selector 2> | <expression 2> |
    |      ..      |       ..       |
    | <selector n> | <expression n> |
  ```

  <p>
    Binds primary and fallback selectors for a web element to the current scope with a default lookup timeout that can be overridden with the `@Timeout` annotation.
    Lookups will be attempted in the order specified until one succeeds.
  </p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;selector n&gt;</code> is the nth selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression n&gt;</code> is the nth selector expression</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1-5}
    Given the todo field can be located by
          | selector | expression  |
          | name     | todo-field  |
          | css      | .todo input |
          | class    | new-todo    |
     When I type "Feed the cat" in the todo field
  ```

  With explicit timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {1-5}
    Given @Timeout('8s') the todo field can be located by
          | selector | expression  |
          | name     | todo-field  |
          | css      | .todo input |
          | class    | new-todo    |
     When I type "Feed the cat" in the todo field
  ```

  Without any timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {1-5}
    Given @Timeout('0s') the todo field can be located by
          | selector | expression  |
          | name     | todo-field  |
          | css      | .todo input |
          | class    | new-todo    |
     When I type "Feed the cat" in the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-with-fallbacks">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.11.0">v2.11.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-with-fallbacks-at-index">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located at index <index> by
    | selector     | expression     |
    | <selector 1> | <expression 1> |
    | <selector 2> | <expression 2> |
    |      ..      |       ..       |
    | <selector n> | <expression n> |
  ```

  <p>
    Binds indexed primary and fallback selectors for a web element to the current scope with a default lookup timeout that can be overridden with the `@Timeout` annotation.
    Lookups will be attempted in the order specified until one succeeds.
  </p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;selector n&gt;</code> is the nth selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression n&gt;</code> is the nth selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;index&gt;</code> is the index of the element to select in list returned by <code>&lt;expression n&gt;</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1-5}
    Given the second item can be located at index 1 by
          | selector | expression       |
          | name     | todo-label       |
          | class    | todo-label       |
          | css      | .todo-list label |
     Then the second item should contain "Feed the cat"
  ```

  With explicit timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {1-5}
    Given @Timeout('9s') the second item can be located at index 1 by
          | selector | expression       |
          | name     | todo-label       |
          | class    | todo-label       |
          | css      | .todo-list label |
     Then the second item should contain "Feed the cat"
  ```

  Without any timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {1-5}
    Given @Timeout('0s') the second item can be located at index 1 by
          | selector | expression       |
          | name     | todo-label       |
          | class    | todo-label       |
          | css      | .todo-list label |
     Then the second item should contain "Feed the cat"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-with-fallbacks-at-index">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.28.0">v2.28.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

##### Relative Locators

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-relative-to-other-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" <relativeTo> <otherElement>
  ```

  <p>Binds a selector for a web element (relative to another) to the current scope with a default lookup timeout that can be overridden with the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;relativeTo&gt;</code> is one of
      <ul>
        <li><code>in</code> to select element contained in <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
        <li>
          Or since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.0.0">v3.0.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><code>above</code> to select element above <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>below</code> to select element below <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>to left of</code> to select element to the left of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>to right of</code> to select element to the right of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>near</code> to select element near <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li>
              <code>near and within &lt;noOfPixels&gt; pixel[s] of</code> to select element near and within a given number of pixels of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code>
              <ul>
                <li>Where <code>&lt;noOfPixels&gt;</code> is a postive integer denoting a number of pixels (max proximity to <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code>)</li>
              </ul>
            </li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code> is the name of the web element that this one is relative to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the button can be located by tag "button"
      And the left field can be located by css "input" to left of the button 
     When I navigate to "https://chercher.tech/practice/relative-locators"
      And I type "I am left of the button" in the left field
     Then the left field should contain "I am left of the button"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-relative-to-other-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.1.0">v1.1.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Settings overrides

<details id="my-name-setting-is-value">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  my <name> setting is "<value>"
  ```
  <p> Overrides a Gwen setting.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is name of the setting to override</li>
    <li><code>&lt;value&gt;</code> is the value to set</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Notes</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      Or as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.21.0">v2.21.0</Link>, this DSL stores all values as thread local settings (instead of system properties).
      <ul>
        <li>This supports different settings for different features in the case of parallel execution.</li>
        <li>Settings loaded from properties files and system properties at startup time are not replaced, but can be overridden with values set here.</li>
        <li>Setting arbitrary system properties (that is: non Gwen settings that do not start with <code>gwen.</code>) is not supported.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>Prior to <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.21.0">v2.21.0</Link>, this DSL stored all values as JVM-global system properties and caution was advised because race conditions could occur if multiple features changed the same system property.</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    Given my gwen.web.useragent setting is "I am robot"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#my-name-setting-is-value">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-reset-my-name-setting">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I reset my <name> setting
  ```
  <p> Resets a Gwen setting to remove a previous override.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;setting&gt;</code> is name of the setting to reset</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    Given I reset my gwen.web.useragent setting
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-reset-my-name-setting">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.21.0">v2.21.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

### Capture

#### Text capture

<details id="i-capture-text-ref-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <textRef> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the referenced text and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the username is "Gwen"
     When I capture the username as my username
     Then my username should be the username
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-text-ref-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <element>
  ```
  <p>Captures the text value of an element and binds it to the element name in the global scode.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to capture the text of</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I capture the heading
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-element-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <element> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the text value of an element and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to capture the text of</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I capture the heading as my heading
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-element-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-name-of-element-by-javascript-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <name> <of|on|in> <element> by <javascript|js> "<script>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a JavaScript expression or function on an element and binds the result to the given name.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the javascript return value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;of|on|in&gt;</code> is <code>of</code>, <code>on</code> or <code>in</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to execute the javascript on</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript|js&gt;</code> is <code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>)</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;script&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or function that will return the value (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>The reference to the element will be provided to the javascript through an implicit object named <code>element</code>.</li>
        <li>For a one liner expression, no function, arrow declaration or <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>
          For a function, use either:
          <ul>
            <li><Link to="/docs/js-functions">Arrow syntax</Link> (preferred): <code>() =&gt; &#123; body &#125;</code> (Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.56.0">v3.56.0</Link>)</li>
            <li>Or anonymous function syntax (legacy): <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code></li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4-11}
    Given the red checkbox can be located by id "red"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I click the red checkbox
      And I capture my favorite color in the red checkbox by js
          """
          () => {
            var color = element.value
            if (!element.checked) color = "Blue"
            return color;
          }
          """
     Then my favorite color should be "Red"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-name-of-element-by-javascript-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Regex capture

<details id="i-capture-the-text-in-text-ref-by-regex-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the text in <textRef> by regex "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the referenced text using the given regex expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the regex selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the date is "2021-09-22"
     When I capture the text in the date by regex "(\d{4})" as the year
     Then the year should be "2021"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-text-in-text-ref-by-regex-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-text-in-element-by-regex-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the text in <element> by regex "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures text content from a web element using the given regex expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to capture text from</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the regex selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # assuming a web element contains date: 2021-09-22
    Given the date field can be located by class "date"
     When I capture the text in the date field by regex "(\d{4})" as the year
     Then the year should be "2021"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-text-in-element-by-regex-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### XPath capture

<details id="i-capture-the-node-type-in-xml-ref-by-xpath-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the <nodeType> in <xmlRef> by xpath "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures XML content from a referenced XML string using the given XPath expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;nodeType&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to capture the text node</li>
        <li><code>node</code> to capture a single node</li>
        <li><code>nodeset</code> to capture multiple nodes</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;xmlRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the XML text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an XML text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the xml is "<result><status>passed</status></result>"
     When I capture the text in the xml by xpath "//result/status" as the status
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-node-type-in-xml-ref-by-xpath-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-node-type-in-element-by-xpath-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the <nodeType> in <element> by xpath "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures XML content from a web element using the given XPath expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;nodeType&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to capture the text node</li>
        <li><code>node</code> to capture a single node</li>
        <li><code>nodeset</code> to capture multiple nodes</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element containing the XML content</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # assuming a web element contains xml: <result><status>passed</status></result>
    Given the xml web element can be located by id "xml"
     When I capture the text in the xml web element by xpath "//result/status" as the status
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-node-type-in-element-by-xpath-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### JSON capture

<details id="i-capture-the-content-in-json-ref-by-json-path-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the content in <jsonRef> by json path "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures JSON content from a referenced JSON string using the given JSON Path expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;jsonRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the source JSON source
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a JSON text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON selector</Link> expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the json is "{ "status": "passed" }"
     When I capture the content in the json by json path "$.status" as the status
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-content-in-json-ref-by-json-path-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Similarity capture

<details id="i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-compared-to-text-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the similarity score of <textRef> compared to "<text>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Compares a text reference with a text value for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm and binds the calculated score to <code>name</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing a text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> is the text to compare <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> against</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the calculated score to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2-4}
    Given the phrase is "Hello world!"
     When I capture the similarity score of the phrase compared to "Hello world" as similarity score 1
      And I capture the similarity score of the phrase compared to "hello world" as similarity score 2
      And @IgnoreCase I capture the similarity score of the phrase compared to "hello world" as similarity score 3
     Then similarity score 1 should be "0.9411764705882353"
      And similarity score 2 should be "0.8235294117647058"
      And similarity score 3 should be "0.9411764705882353"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-compared-to-text-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.0">v3.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-1-compared-to-text-ref-2-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the similarity score of <textRef1> compared to <textRef2> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Compares a text reference with another for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm and binds the calculated score to <code>name</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef1&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing a text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef2&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the second text reference to compare &lt;textRef1&gt; against
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the calculated score to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3-4}
    Given phrase 1 is "Hello world!"
      And phrase 2 is "hello world"
     When I capture the similarity score of phrase 1 compared to phrase 2 as similarity score 1
      And @IgnoreCase I capture the similarity score of phrase 1 compared to phrase 2 as similarity score 2
     Then similarity score 1 should be "0.8235294117647058"
      And similarity score 2 should be "0.9411764705882353"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-1-compared-to-text-ref-2-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.0">v3.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-compared-to-text">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the similarity score of <textRef> compared to "<text>"
  ```
  <p>Compares a text reference with a text value for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm and binds the calculated score to the <code>similarity score</code> attribute in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing a text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> is the text to compare <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> against</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the phrase is "Hello world!"
     When I capture the similarity score of the phrase compared to "Hello world"
     Then similarity score should be "0.9411764705882353"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-compared-to-text">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.0">v3.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-1-compared-to-text-ref-2">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the similarity score of <textRef1> compared to <textRef2>
  ```
  <p>Compares a text reference with another for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm and binds the calculated score to the <code>similarity score</code> attribute in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef1&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing a text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef2&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the second text reference to compare &lt;textRef1&gt; against
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}

      And phrase 2 is "hello world"
     When I capture the similarity score of phrase 1 compared to phrase 2
     Then similarity score should be "0.8235294117647058"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">

#### PDF capture

<details id="i-capture-pdf-text-from-the-current-url">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the PDF text from the current URL
  ```
  <p>Captures the text in a PDF document from the current URL in the browser and binds it to <code>the PDF text</code> variable in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the pdf url is "https://example.com/file.pdf"
     When I navigate to "${the pdf url}"
      And I capture the PDF text from the current URL
     Then the PDF text should contain "Some expected text"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-pdf-text-from-the-current-url">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.53.0">v3.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>


<details id="i-capture-pdf-text-from-the-current-url-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the PDF text from the current URL as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the text in a PDF document from the current URL in the browser and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name in the global scope to bind the captured PDF text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the pdf url is "https://example.com/file.pdf"
     When I navigate to "${the pdf url}"
      And I capture the PDF text from the current URL as content
     Then content should contain "Some expected text"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-pdf-text-from-the-current-url-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.53.0">v3.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

  <p>Captures the text in a PDF document from a given URL location and binds it to <code>the PDF text</code> variable in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;url&gt;</code> is the web URL of the PDF document to capture the text of</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}

     Then the PDF text should contain "Some expected text"
  ```
