#### Base64 capture

<details id="i-base64-decode-text-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I base64 decode <textRef>
  ```
  <p>Base64 decodes the text reference and binds the result to the same name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to decode
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the data is "c29tZSBiaW5hcnkgZGF0YQ=="
     When I base64 decode the data
     Then the data should be "some binary data"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-base64-decode-text-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-base64-decode-text-ref-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I base64 decode <textRef> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Base64 decodes the text reference and binds the result to the give name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to decode
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the decoded value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the encoded data is "c29tZSBiaW5hcnkgZGF0YQ=="
     When I base64 decode the encoded data as the decoded data
     Then the decoded data should be "some binary data"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-base64-decode-text-ref-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-base64-decode-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I base64 decode <element>
  ```
  <p>Base64 decodes the text in the given element and binds the result to the same name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element containing the text to decode</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the data can be located by class "encoded-data"
     When I base64 decode the data
     Then the data should be "some binary data"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-base64-decode-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-base64-decode-element-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I base64 decode <element> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Base64 decodes the text in the given element and binds the result to the give name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element containing the text to decode</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the decoded value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the encoded data field can be located by class "encoded-data"
     When I base64 decode the encoded data as the decoded data
     Then the decoded data should be "some binary data"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-base64-decode-element-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### URL capture
<details id="i-capture-the-current-url">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the current URL
  ```
  
  <p>Captures the current browser URL and binds it as <code>the current URL</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    When I capture the current URL
     And I navigate to "${the current URL}?q=gwen"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-current-url">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-current-url-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the current URL as <name>
  ```
  
  <p>Captures the current browser URL and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured URL to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    When I capture the current URL as the base URL
     And I navigate to "${the base URL}?q=gwen"
    Then the current URL should start with the base URL
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-current-url-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-text-in-the-current-url-by-regex-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the text in the current URL by regex "<expression>" as <name>
  ```

  <p>Extracts a substring from the current browser URL using the given regex and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the regex expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured substring to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    When I capture the text in the current URL by regex "q=([^&]*)" as q
    Then q should be "gwen"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-text-in-the-current-url-by-regex-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Dropdown capture

<details id="i-capture-dropdown">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <dropdown> <text|value>
  ```
  <p>Captures the selected text or value of a dropdown element and binds it to the element name in the global scode.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element to capture the text or value of</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to captured the displayed text of the selection</li>
        <li><code>value</code> to captured the option value of the selection</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I capture the age dropdown text
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-dropdown">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-dropdown-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <dropdown> <text|value> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the selected text or value of a dropdown element and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element to capture the text or value of</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to captured the displayed text of the selection</li>
        <li><code>value</code> to captured the option value of the selection</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I capture the age dropdown text my age
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-dropdown-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Screenshot capture

<details id="i-capture-the-current-screenshot">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the current screenshot
  ```
  <p>Captures the current screenshot and attaches it to the Gwen report.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I capture the current screenshot
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-current-screenshot">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.6.0">v1.6.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-current-screenshot-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the current screenshot as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the current screenshot, attaches it to the Gwen report, and binds the filepath of the saved image to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> the name to bind the captured image filepath to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I capture the current screenshot as the screenshot image
     Then the screenshot image should contain "path/to/image.png"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-current-screenshot-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.49.0">v2.49.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Element capture

<details id="i-capture-element-screenshot-of-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture element screenshot of <element>
  ```
  <p>Captures the screenshot of a web element and attaches it to the Gwen report.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> the name of the web element to capture the screenshot of</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I type "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I capture element screenshot of the todo field
  ```

<details id="i-capture-element-screenshot-of-element-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture element screenshot of <element> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the screenshot of a web element, attaches it to the Gwen report, and binds the filepath of the saved image to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> the name of the web element to capture the screenshot of</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> the name to bind the captured image filepath to</li>
  </ul>

  ```gherkin {4}
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I type "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I capture element screenshot of the todo field as my element screenshot
  ```

  </div>
</details>

#### Data lookups

<details id="i-lookup-name-in-the-filepath-file-where-filter">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I lookup <name> in the "<filepath>" file where "<predicate>"
  ```
  <p>Looks up a named data value in a CSV or JSON file based on a predicate function and binds its value to the same name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code>the name of the data to look up the value of and the name to bind it to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the CSV or JSON file to look up</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;predicate&gt;</code> is the javascript predicate expression that will return <code>true</code> when a match is found for a record or <code>false</code> otherwise (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      Data fields can be referenced in the predicate using either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>$&#123;data.record.NAME&#125;</code> (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.47.0">v3.47.0</Link>)</li>
        <li><code>$&#123;csv.record.NAME&#125;</code> for CSV data or <code>$&#123;json.record.NAME&#125;</code> for JSON data (for prior versions)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>

  The data value contained in the first record that satisifes the given predicate will be bound to the global scope. Otherwise if no records match, then no value will be bound.

  <p>Examples</p>

  ##### CSV Lookup

  Given the CSV file: lookup/StateCodes.csv

  ```csv {9}
  Code,Name
  ACT,Australian Capital Territory
  NSW,New South Wales
  NT,Northern Territory
  QLD,Queensland
  SA,South Australia
  TAS,Tasmania
  VIC,Victoria
  WA,Western Australia
  ```

  The following will bind "Western Australia" in the last record to <code>Name</code> in the global scope

  ```gherkin {1}
    When I lookup Name in the "lookup/StateCodes.csv" file where "'${data.record.Code}' == 'WA'"
    Then Name should be "Western Australia"
  ```

  ##### JSON Lookup
 
  > Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.47.0">v3.47.0</Link>

  Given the JSON file: lookup/StateCodes.json

  ```json {5}
  [
    { "Code": "ACT", "Name": "Australian Capital Territory" },
    { "Code": "NSW", "Name": "New South Wales" },
    { "Code": "NT",  "Name": "Northern Territory" },
    { "Code": "QLD", "Name": "Queensland" },
    { "Code": "SA",  "Name": "South Australia" },
    { "Code": "TAS", "Name": "Tasmania" },
    { "Code": "VIC", "Name": "Victoria" },
    { "Code": "WA",  "Name": "Western Australia" }
  ]
  ```

  The following will bind "Western Australia" in the last record to <code>Name</code> in the global scope

  ```gherkin {1}
    When I lookup Name in the "lookup/StateCodes.json" file where "'${data.record.Code}' == 'WA'"
    Then Name should be "Western Australia"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-lookup-name-in-the-filepath-file-where-filter">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.30.0">v3.30.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-lookup-name-in-the-filepath-ref-file-where-filter">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I lookup <name> in <filepathRef file> where "<predicate>"
  ```
  <p>Looks up a named data value in a referenced CSV or JSON file based on a predicate function and binds its value to the same name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code>the name of the data to look up the value of and the name to bind it to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the CSV or JSON file to look up</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;predicate&gt;</code> is the javascript predicate expression that will return <code>true</code> when a match is found for a record or <code>false</code> otherwise (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      Data fields can be referenced in the predicate using either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>$&#123;data.record.NAME&#125;</code> (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.47.0">v3.47.0</Link>)</li>
        <li><code>$&#123;csv.record.NAME&#125;</code> for CSV data or <code>$&#123;json.record.NAME&#125;</code> for JSON data (for prior versions)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>

  The data value contained in the first record that satisifes the given predicate will be bound to the global scope. Otherwise if no records match, then no value will be bound.

  <p>Examples</p>

  ##### CSV Lookup

  Given the CSV file: lookup/StateCodes.csv

  ```csv {5}
  Code,Name
  ACT,Australian Capital Territory
  NSW,New South Wales
  NT,Northern Territory
  QLD,Queensland
  SA,South Australia
  TAS,Tasmania
  VIC,Victoria
  WA,Western Australia
  ```

  The following will bind "QLD" in the 4th record to <code>Code</code> in the global scope

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given mapping file is "lookup/StateCodes.csv"
     When I lookup Code in mapping file where "'${data.record.Name}' == 'Queensland'"
     Then Code should be "QLD"
  ```

  ##### JSON Lookup
 
  > Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.47.0">v3.47.0</Link>

  Given the JSON file: lookup/StateCodes.json

  ```json {5}
  [
    { "Code": "ACT", "Name": "Australian Capital Territory" },
    { "Code": "NSW", "Name": "New South Wales" },
    { "Code": "NT",  "Name": "Northern Territory" },
    { "Code": "QLD", "Name": "Queensland" },
    { "Code": "SA",  "Name": "South Australia" },
    { "Code": "TAS", "Name": "Tasmania" },
    { "Code": "VIC", "Name": "Victoria" },
    { "Code": "WA",  "Name": "Western Australia" }
  ]
  ```

  The following will bind "QLD" in the 4th record to <code>Code</code> in the global scope

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given mapping file is "lookup/StateCodes.json"
     When I lookup Code in mapping file where "'${data.record.Name}' == 'Queensland'"
     Then Code should be "QLD"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-lookup-name-in-the-filepath-ref-file-where-filter">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.30.0">v3.30.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-lookup-column-in-the-filepath-file-as-name-where-filter">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I lookup <dataName> in the "<filepath>" file as <name> where "<predicate>"
  ```
  <p>Looks up a named data value in a CSV or JSON file based on a predicate function and binds its value to a given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dataName&gt;</code> the name of the data to look up the value of</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the CSV or JSON file to look up</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> the name to bind the looked up value to in the global scope</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;predicate&gt;</code> is the javascript predicate expression that will return <code>true</code> when a match is found for a record or <code>false</code> otherwise (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      Data fields can be referenced in the predicate using either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>$&#123;data.record.NAME&#125;</code> (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.47.0">v3.47.0</Link>)</li>
        <li><code>$&#123;csv.record.NAME&#125;</code> for CSV data or <code>$&#123;json.record.NAME&#125;</code> for JSON data (for prior versions)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>

  The data value contained in the first record that satisifes the given predicate will be bound to the global scope. Otherwise if no records match, then no value will be bound.

  <p>Examples</p>

  ##### CSV Lookup

  Given the CSV file: lookup/StateCodes.csv

  ```csv {3}
  Code,Name
  ACT,Australian Capital Territory
  NSW,New South Wales
  NT,Northern Territory
  QLD,Queensland
  SA,South Australia
  TAS,Tasmania
  VIC,Victoria
  WA,Western Australia
  ```

  The following will bind "New South Wales" in the 2nd record to <code>state name</code> in the global scope

  ```gherkin {1}
    When I lookup Name in the "lookup/StateCodes.csv" file as state name where "'${data.record.Code}' == 'NSW'"
    Then state name should be "New South Wales"
  ```

  ##### JSON Lookup
 
  > Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.47.0">v3.47.0</Link>

  Given the JSON file: lookup/StateCodes.json

  ```json {5}
  [
    { "Code": "ACT", "Name": "Australian Capital Territory" },
    { "Code": "NSW", "Name": "New South Wales" },
    { "Code": "NT",  "Name": "Northern Territory" },
    { "Code": "QLD", "Name": "Queensland" },
    { "Code": "SA",  "Name": "South Australia" },
    { "Code": "TAS", "Name": "Tasmania" },
    { "Code": "VIC", "Name": "Victoria" },
    { "Code": "WA",  "Name": "Western Australia" }
  ]
  ```

  The following will bind "New South Wales" in the 2nd record to <code>state name</code> in the global scope

  ```gherkin {1}
    When I lookup Name in the "lookup/StateCodes.json" file as state name where "'${data.record.Code}' == 'NSW'"
    Then state name should be "New South Wales"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-lookup-column-in-the-filepath-file-as-name-where-filter">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.30.0">v3.30.0</Link></div>

</details>

<details id="i-lookup-column-in-the-filepath-ref-file-as-name-where-filter">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I lookup <dataName> in <filepathRef file> as <name> where "<predicate>"
  ```
  <p>Looks up a named column value in a referenced CSV or JSON file based on a predicate function and binds its value to a given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dataName&gt;</code> the name of the data in the CSV or JSON file to look up the value of</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the CSV or JSON file to look up</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> the name to bind the looked up value to in the global scope</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;predicate&gt;</code> is the javascript predicate expression that will return <code>true</code> when a match is found for a record or <code>false</code> otherwise (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      Data fields can be referenced in the predicate using either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>$&#123;data.record.NAME&#125;</code> (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.47.0">v3.47.0</Link>)</li>
        <li><code>$&#123;csv.record.NAME&#125;</code> for CSV data or <code>$&#123;json.record.NAME&#125;</code> for JSON data (for prior versions)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>

  The data value contained in the first record that satisifes the given predicate will be bound to the global scope. Otherwise if no records match, then no value will be bound.

  <p>Examples</p>

  ##### CSV Lookup

  Given the CSV file: lookup/StateCodes.csv

  ```csv {8}
  Code,Name
  ACT,Australian Capital Territory
  NSW,New South Wales
  NT,Northern Territory
  QLD,Queensland
  SA,South Australia
  TAS,Tasmania
  VIC,Victoria
  WA,Western Australia
  ```

  The following will bind "VIC" in the 7th record to <code>state code</code> in the global scope

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given mapping file is "lookup/StateCodes.csv"
     When I lookup Code in mapping file as state code where "'${data.record.Name}' == 'Victoria'"
     Then state code should be "VIC"
  ```

  ##### JSON Lookup
 
  > Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.47.0">v3.47.0</Link>

  Given the JSON file: lookup/StateCodes.json

  ```json {5}
  [
    { "Code": "ACT", "Name": "Australian Capital Territory" },
    { "Code": "NSW", "Name": "New South Wales" },
    { "Code": "NT",  "Name": "Northern Territory" },
    { "Code": "QLD", "Name": "Queensland" },
    { "Code": "SA",  "Name": "South Australia" },
    { "Code": "TAS", "Name": "Tasmania" },
    { "Code": "VIC", "Name": "Victoria" },
    { "Code": "WA",  "Name": "Western Australia" }
  ]
  ```

### Actions

#### Page actions

<details id="i-navigate-to-url">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I navigate to "<url>"
  ```

  <p>Navigates the browser to the given URL. Starts a new browser window if one is not open.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;url&gt;</code> is the URL to navigate to (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-navigate-to-url">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center">Supports [performance trace](/docs/faq#can-i-log-a-performance-trace) capture (since v4.3.0)</div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I refresh the current page
  ```

  <p>Refreshes the current page in the browser.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I refresh the current page
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">

#### Element actions

<details id="i-click-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <click|right click|double click> <element>
  ```
  <p>Clicks a web element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;click|right click|double click&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>click</code> to click the element</li>
        <li><code>right click</code> to right click the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>double click</code> to double click the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to click</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the start button can be located by name "commit"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
      And I click the start button
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-click-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-click-element-of-context">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <click|right click|double click> <element> of <context>
  ```
  <p>Clicks a context sensitive web element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;click|right click|double click&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>click</code> to click the element</li>
        <li><code>right click</code> to right click the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>double click</code> to double click the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to click</li>
    <li><code>&lt;context&gt;</code> is the context element to focus into (in order to click <code>&lt;element&gt;</code>)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the menu item can be located by id "menu-item-id"
      And the action button can be located by id "action-button-id"
     When I click the action button of the menu item
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-click-element-of-context">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-modifier-keys-click-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <modifierKeys> <click|right click|double click> <element>
  ```
  <p>Holds down the specified modifier keys and clicks an element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;modifierKeys&gt;</code> is a <code>+</code> separated list of modifier keys to hold down during the click
      <ul>
        <li>Modifier keys can be single keyboard characters or any supported <Link to="https://seleniumhq.github.io/selenium/docs/api/java/org/openqa/selenium/Keys.html">key constants</Link></li>
        <li><i>Node:</i> Keys behave differently on different platforms</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;click|right click|double click&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>click</code> to click the element</li>
        <li><code>right click</code> to right click the element</li>
        <li><code>double click</code> to double click the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to click</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the button can be located by tag "button"
      And I COMMAND+SHIFT click the button
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-modifier-keys-click-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-tick-or-until-checkbox">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <check|uncheck|tick|untick> <checkbox>
  ```
  <p>Ticks or unticks a checkbox element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;check|uncheck|tick|untick&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>check</code> (or <code>tick</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to tick the checkbox element</li>
        <li><code>uncheck</code> (or <code>untick</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to untick the checkbox element</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;checkbox&gt;</code> is the name of the checkbox element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the email checkbox can be located by id "checkbox1"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I tick the email checkbox
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-tick-or-until-checkbox">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-move-to-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I move to <element>
  ```
  <p>Moves to a web element and gives it the focus.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to move to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the surname field can be located by id "surname"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I move to the surname field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-move-to-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-enter-or-type-text-in-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <enter|type> "<text>" in <element>
  ```
  <p>Enters or types text into a web element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;enter|type&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>enter</code> to send the text to the field followed by the enter key</li>
        <li><code>type</code> to send the text to the field only (without trailing enter key)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> is the text to send to the field</li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the field to send the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-enter-or-type-text-in-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-enter-or-type-text-ref-in-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <enter|type> <textRef> in <element>
  ```
  <p>Enters or types a text reference value into a web element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;enter|type&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>enter</code> to send the text to the field followed by the enter key</li>
        <li><code>type</code> to send the text to the field only (without trailing enter key)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to send to the field
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the field to send the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my item is "Walk the dog"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter my item in the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-enter-or-type-text-ref-in-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-append-text-to-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I append "<text>" to <element>
  ```
  <p>Appends the given text to the current text value of an element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> is the text to append</li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is name of the element to append the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the search field can be located by name "q"
     When I navigate to "https://google.com"
      And I type "Gwen" in the search field
      And I append " automation" to the search field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-append-text-to-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.18.0">v2.18.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-append-text-ref-to-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I append <textRef> to <element>
  ```
  <p>Appends the given referenced text to the current text value of an element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to append to the element
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is name of the element to append the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the search field can be located by name "q"
      And my additional search term is " automation"
     When I navigate to "https://google.com"
      And I type "Gwen" in the search field
      And I append my additional search term to the search field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-append-text-ref-to-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.18.0">v2.18.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-press-enter-or-tab-in-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I press <enter|tab> in <element>
  ```
  <p>Send the enter or tab key to a web element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;enter|tab&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>enter</code> to send the enter key</li>
        <li><code>tab</code> to send the tab key</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to send the key to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the surname field can be located by id "surname"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I press tab in the surname field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-press-enter-or-tab-in-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-send-keys-to-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I send "<keys>" to <element>
  ```
  <p>Sends a sequence of keys to an element (for emulating keyboard shortcuts).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;keys&gt;</code> is a <code>,</code> or <code>+</code> (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link>) separated list of keys to send.
      <ul>
        <li>Keys can be single keyboard characters or any supported <Link to="https://seleniumhq.github.io/selenium/docs/api/java/org/openqa/selenium/Keys.html">key constants</Link></li>
        <li><i>Note:</i> Keys behave differently on different platforms</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to send the keys to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4,5,7,8}
    Given the search field can be located by name "q"
     When I navigate to "https://google.com"
      And I type "automation" in the search field
      And I send "COMMAND+A" to the search field
      And I send "COMMAND+C" to the search field
      And I clear the search field
      And I send "COMMAND+V" to the search field
      And I send "ARROW_DOWN" to the search field
      And I press enter in the search field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-send-keys-to-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-insert-a-new-line-in-textarea">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I insert a new line in <textarea>
  ```
  <p>Inserts a new line into a textarea element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textarea&gt;</code> is the name of the textarea element to insert the new line into</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4,6}
    Given the more field can be located by tag "textarea"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I type "Hi," in the more field
      And I insert a new line in the more field
      And I type "I like Gwen." in the more field
      And I insert a new line in the more field
      And I type "Bye!" in the more field
     Then the more field should contain
          """
          Hi,
          I like Gwen.
          Bye!
          """
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-insert-a-new-line-in-textarea">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.19.0">v2.19.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I clear <element>
  ```
  <p>Clears a text element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to clear</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the surname field can be located by id "surname"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I clear the surname field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-clear-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>

  </div>
</details>

#### Dropdown actions

<details id="i-select-or-deselect-the-position-option-in-dropdown">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <select|deselect> the <position><st|nd|rd|th> option in <dropdown>
  ```
  <p>Selects an option in a dropdown by position.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;select|deselect&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>select</code> to select the option</li>
        <li>
          <code>deselect</code> to deselect the option, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><i>Note</i>: Deselect will only work for multi-select dropdowns.</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;position&gt;</code> is the position number of the option(1 for first position)</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;st|nd|rd|th&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>st</code> if the position number ends in 1</li>
        <li><code>nd</code> if the position number ends in 2</li>
        <li><code>rd</code> if the position number ends in 3</li>
        <li><code>th</code> if the position number is greater than 3</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select the 2nd option in the age dropdown
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-select-or-deselect-the-position-option-in-dropdown">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-select-or-deselect-option-in-dropdown">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <select|deselect> "<option>" in <dropdown>
  ```
  <p>Selects an option in a dropdown by displayed text.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;select|deselect&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>select</code> to select the option</li>
        <li>
          <code>deselect</code> to deselect the option, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><i>Note</i>: Deselect will only work for multi-select dropdowns.</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;option&gt;</code> is the displayed option text</li>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select "18" in the age dropdown
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-select-or-deselect-option-in-dropdown">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-select-or-deselect-option-ref-in-dropdown">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <select|deselect> <optionRef> in <dropdown>
  ```
  <p>Selects an option in a dropdown by a displayed text reference.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;select|deselect&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>select</code> to select the option</li>
        <li>
          <code>deselect</code> to deselect the option, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><i>Note</i>: Deselect will only work for multi-select dropdowns.</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;optionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the displayed option text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
      And my age is "24"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select my age in the age dropdown
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-select-or-deselect-option-ref-in-dropdown">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-select-or-deselect-option-in-dropdown-by-value">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <select|deselect> "<option>" in <dropdown> by value
  ```
  <p>Selects an option in a dropdown by hidden value.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;select|deselect&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>select</code> to select the option</li>
        <li>
          <code>deselect</code> to deselect the option, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><i>Note</i>: Deselect will only work for multi-select dropdowns.</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;option&gt;</code> is the hidden option value</li>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select "21" in the age dropdown by value
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-select-or-deselect-option-in-dropdown-by-value">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-select-or-deselect-option-ref-in-dropdown-by-value">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <select|deselect> <optionRef> in <dropdown> by value
  ```
  <p>Selects an option in a dropdown by hidden value reference.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;select|deselect&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>select</code> to select the option</li>
        <li>
          <code>deselect</code> to deselect the option, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><i>Note</i>: Deselect will only work for multi-select dropdowns.</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;optionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the hidden option value
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
      And the age is "24"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I deselect the age in the age dropdown
  ```

#### Form actions

<details id="i-submit-form">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I submit <form>
  ```

  </summary>

#### Window and tab actions

<details id="i-have-an-open-browser">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I have an open browser
  ```
  <p>Opens a browser if none are open</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given I have an open browser
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     Then I should have 1 open browser
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-have-an-open-browser">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.41.0">v2.41.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-have-no-open-browser">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I have no open browser
  ```
  <p>Closes all open browsers</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given I have no open browser
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     Then I should have 1 open browser
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-have-no-open-browser">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.41.0">v2.41.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-start-a-new-browser">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I start a new browser
  ```
  <p>Starts a new browser session (or switches to exising one if it is already open).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
   Given I have no open browser
    When I start a new browser
    Then I should have 1 open browser
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-start-a-new-browser">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-close-the-current-browser">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I close the[ current] browser
  ```
  <p>Closes the current browser session (or does nothing if one is not open).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>[ current]</code> including the word <code>current</code> is optional and makes no difference, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.3.0">v1.3.0</Link></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2,4}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     And I close the current browser
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/vue/"
     And I close the browser
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-close-the-current-browser">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-start-a-browser-for-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I start a browser for <name>
  ```
  <p>Starts a new browser session with the given name (closes any existing browser of that name first).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is a name assigned to the browser session</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1,3}
    When I start a browser for React
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     And I start a browser for Vue
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/vue/"
    Then I should have 2 open browsers
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-start-a-browser-for-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to <name>
  ```
  <p>Switches to a named browser session (starts a new browser if one of that name is not already open). All browser actions performed after this will execute in the named session.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the browser session to switch to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    When I start a browser for React
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     And I start a browser for Vue
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/vue/"
     And I switch to React
    Then the current URL should contain "react"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-close-the-browser-for-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I close the browser for <name>
  ```
  <p>Closes a named browser session (does nothing if one of that name is not open).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the browser session to close</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    When I start a browser for React
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     And I close the browser for React
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-close-the-browser-for-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-start-a-new-browser-tab-or-window">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I start a new browser <tab|window>
  ```
  <p>Starts a new browser tab or window (or starts a new browser session if one is not open).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://google.com"
     And I start a new browser tab
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-start-a-new-browser-tab-or-window">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.0.0">v3.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-tab-or-window-occurrence">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to <tab|window> <occurrence>
  ```
  <p>Switches to a previously opened tab or window occurrence.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;occurrence&gt;</code> is the tab or window occurrence to switch to (1st opened is occurrence 1, 2nd is 2, ..)
      <ul>
        <li><em>Note:</em> the occurrence number of the default tab/window in a new browser session is 0</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    When I navigate to "https://google.com"
     And I start a new browser tab
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     And I switch to window 1
    Then the page title should contain "Google"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-tab-or-window-occurrence">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.0.0">v3.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-close-tab-or-window-occurrence">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I close <tab|window> <occurrence>
  ```
  <p>Closes a previously opened tab or window occurrence.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;occurrence&gt;</code> is the tab or window occurrence to close to (1st opened is occurrence 1, 2nd is 2, ..)
      <ul>
        <li><em>Note:</em> you cannot close the default tab/window opened by starting a new browser session with this DSL. Use <Link to="#i-close-the-current-browser"><code>I close the[ current] browser</code></Link> instead in that case.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    When I navigate to "https://google.com"
     And I start a new browser tab
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     And I close tab 1
    Then the page title should contain "Google"
  ```
  
  If used in conjunction with <Link to="/docs/try-steps"><code>@Try</code></Link>, will switch to the parent window regardless of whether or not a tab or window was closed (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.4">3.12.4</Link>).
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-close-tab-or-window-occurrence">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.0.0">v3.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-the-child-tab-or-window">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to the child <tab|window>
  ```
  <p>Switches to the most recently opened child tab or window (without closing the parent window)</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the new window button can be located by name "newbrowserwindow123"
     When I navigate to "https://nxtgenaiacademy.com/multiplewindows/"
      And I click the new window button
      And I switch to the child window
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-the-child-tab-or-window">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-close-the-child-tab-or-window">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I close the child <tab|window>
  ```
  <p>Closes the currently active child tab or window and passes control back to the parent window.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the new tab button can be located by name "newbrowsertab453"
     When I navigate to "https://nxtgenaiacademy.com/multiplewindows/"
      And I click the new tab button
      And I switch to the child tab
      And I close the child tab
  ```
  
  If used in conjunction with <Link to="/docs/try-steps"><code>@Try</code></Link>, will switch to the parent window regardless of whether or not a child window was closed (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.4">3.12.4</Link>).
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-close-the-child-tab-or-window">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-child-tab-or-window-occurrence">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to child <tab|window> <occurrence>
  ```
  <p>Switches to a child tab or window occurrence (without closing the parent window) or reports and error if there is no child window.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;occurrence&gt;</code> is the tab or window occurrence to switch to (1st opened is occurrence 1, 2nd is 2, ..)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the new window button can be located by name "newbrowserwindow123"
     When I navigate to "https://nxtgenaiacademy.com/multiplewindows/"
      And I click the new window button
      And I switch to child window 1
  ```
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-child-tab-or-window-occurrence">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.49.0">v2.49.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-close-child-tab-or-window-occurrence">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I close child <tab|window> <occurrence>
  ```
  <p>Closes a child tab or window occurrence and passes control back to the parent window.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;occurrence&gt;</code> is the tab or window occurrence to close (1st opened is occurrence 1, 2nd is 2, ..)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the new tab button can be located by name "newbrowsertab453"
     When I navigate to "https://nxtgenaiacademy.com/multiplewindows/"
      And I click the new tab button
      And I switch to child tab 1
      And I close child tab 1
  ```

  If used in conjunction with <Link to="/docs/try-steps"><code>@Try</code></Link>, will switch to the parent window regardless of whether or not a child window was closed (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.4">3.12.4</Link>).
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-close-child-tab-or-window-occurrence">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.49.0">v2.49.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-the-parent-tab-or-window">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to the parent <tab|window>
  ```
  <p>Switches to the parent window of the currently active window (without closing the currently active window) or stays on the root window if there is no other window open.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the new window button can be located by name "newbrowserwindow123"
     When I navigate to "https://nxtgenaiacademy.com/multiplewindows/"
      And I click the new window button
      And I switch to child window 1
      And I switch to the parent window
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-the-parent-tab-or-window">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-the-root-tab-or-window">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to the root <tab|window>
  ```
  <p>Switches to the topmost parent window (without closing the currently active window) or stays on the current window if it is the root window.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the new window button can be located by name "newbrowserwindow123"
     When I navigate to "https://nxtgenaiacademy.com/multiplewindows/"
      And I click the new window button
      And I switch to child window 1
      And I switch to the root window
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-the-root-tab-or-window">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.14.0">v4.14.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-maximize-the-window">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <maximize|maximise> the window
  ```
  <p>Maximizes the currently active browser window to fill the entire screen area.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;maximize|maximise&gt;</code> is either <code>maximize</code> or <code>maximise</code> (makes no difference)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     And I maximize the window
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-maximize-the-window">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.2.0">v2.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-resize-the-window-to-width-w-and-height-h">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I resize the window to width <w> and height <h>
  ```
  <p>Resizes the currently active browser window to the given dimensions.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;w&gt;</code> is the width in pixels</li>
    <li><code>&lt;h&gt;</code> is the height in pixels</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     And I resize the window to width 1280 and height 720
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-resize-the-window-to-width-w-and-height-h">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.2.0">v2.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-send-keys">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I send "<keys>"
  ```
  <p>Sends a sequence of keys to the browser (for emulating keyboard shortcuts).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;keys&gt;</code> is a <code>,</code> or <code>+</code> (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link>) separated list of keys to send.
      <ul>
        <li>Keys can be single keyboard characters or any supported <Link to="https://seleniumhq.github.io/selenium/docs/api/java/org/openqa/selenium/Keys.html">key constants</Link></li>
        <li><i>Note:</i> Keys behave differently on different platforms</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
     When I navigate to "https://google.com"
      And I send "COMMAND+t"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-send-keys">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.44.0">v2.44.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-set-the-window-position-to-x-and-y">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I set the window position to x <x> and y <y>
  ```
  <p>Positions the currently active browser window to the given co-ordinates.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;x&gt;</code> is the x co-ordinate</li>
    <li><code>&lt;y&gt;</code> is the y co-ordinate</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     And I set the window position to x 40 and y 20
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-set-the-window-position-to-x-and-y">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.7.0">v4.7.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-send-keys">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I send "<keys>"
  ```
  <p>Sends a sequence of keys to the browser (for emulating keyboard shortcuts).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;keys&gt;</code> is a <code>,</code> or <code>+</code> (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link>) separated list of keys to send.
      <ul>
        <li>Keys can be single keyboard characters or any supported <Link to="https://seleniumhq.github.io/selenium/docs/api/java/org/openqa/selenium/Keys.html">key constants</Link></li>
        <li><i>Note:</i> Keys behave differently on different platforms</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
     When I navigate to "https://google.com"
  ```
