#### Frame actions

<details id="i-switch-to-the-default-content">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to the default content
  ```
  <p>Switches to either the first frame on the page, or the main document when a page contains iframes.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://page-with-iframes"
     And I switch to the default content
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-the-default-content">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-frame-content">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to <frame> content
  ```
  <p>Switches the context to a frame.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;frame&gt;</code> is a frame binding name
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
   Given the frame can be located by id "frame_id"
    When I navigate to "https://page-with-iframes"
     And I switch to the frame content
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-frame-content">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.72.0">v2.72.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Alert and Popup actions

<details id="i-accept-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I accept the <alert|confirmation> popup
  ```
  <p>Accepts and closes an alert or confirmation popup by clicking OK.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;alert|confirmation&gt;</code> is either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>alert</code> for an alert box with an OK button</li>
        <li><code>confirmation</code> for a confirmation box with OK and Cancel buttons</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the alert link can be located by id "alert"
     When I navigate to "https://www.selenium.dev/selenium/web/alerts.html"
      And I click the alert link
      And I accept the alert popup
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-accept-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-dismiss-the-confirmation-popup">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I dismiss the confirmation popup
  ```
  <p>Dismisses and closes a confirmation popup by clicking Cancel.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the confirmation link can be located by id "prompt-with-default"
     When I navigate to "https://www.selenium.dev/selenium/web/alerts.html"
      And I click the confirmation link
      And I dismiss the confirmation popup
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-dismiss-the-confirmation-popup">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the <alert|confirmation> popup message
  ```
  <p>Captures the alert or confirmation popup message and binds it to <code>the &lt;alert|confirmation&gt; popup message</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;alert|confirmation&gt;</code> is either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>alert</code> for an alert box with an OK button</li>
        <li><code>confirmation</code> for a confirmation box with OK and Cancel buttons</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the alert link can be located by id "alert"
     When I navigate to "https://www.selenium.dev/selenium/web/alerts.html"
      And I click the alert link
      And I capture the alert popup message
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.24.0">v2.24.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the <alert|confirmation> popup message as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the alert or confirmation popup message and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;alert|confirmation&gt;</code> is either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>alert</code> for an alert box with an OK button</li>
        <li><code>confirmation</code> for a confirmation box with OK and Cancel buttons</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the confirmation link can be located by id "prompt-with-default"
     When I navigate to "https://www.selenium.dev/selenium/web/alerts.html"
      And I click the confirmation link
      And I capture the confirmation popup message as the alert message
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.24.0">v2.24.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Scroll actions

<details id="i-scroll-to-the-top-or-bottom-of-page">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I scroll to the <top|bottom> of the page
  ```
  <p>Scrolls to the top or bottom of the current page.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;top|bottom&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>top</code> to scroll to the top of the page</li>
        <li><code>bottom</code> to scroll to the bottom of the page</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I scroll to the bottom of the page
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-scroll-to-the-top-or-bottom-of-page">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.20.1">v3.20.1</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-scroll-to-the-top-or-bottom-of-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I scroll to the <top|bottom> of <element>
  ```
  <p>Scrolls to the top or bottom of the given element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;top|bottom&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>top</code> to scroll to the top of the element</li>
        <li><code>bottom</code> to scroll to the bottom of the element</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> the name of the element to scroll to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the surname field can be located by id "surname"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I scroll to the top of the surname field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-scroll-to-the-top-or-bottom-of-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Drag Drop actions

<details id="i-drag-and-drop-source-element-to-target-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I drag and drop <sourceElement> to <targetElement>
  ```
  <p>Drags and drops a source element onto a target element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;sourceElement&gt;</code> is the name of the source element to drag</li>
    <li><code>&lt;targetElement&gt;</code> is the name of the target element to drop the <code>&lt;sourceElement&gt;</code> into</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the box can be located by xpath "//*[@id='credit2']/a"
      And the cell can be located by xpath "//*[@id='bank']/li"
     When I navigate to "http://demo.guru99.com/test/drag_drop.html"
      And I capture the box as the box text
      And I drag and drop the box to the cell
     Then the cell should contain "${the box text}"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-drag-and-drop-source-element-to-target-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.17.0">v2.17.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### JS actions

<details id="element-can-be-actioned-by-javascript">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be <actioned> by <javascript|js> "<script>"
  ```
  <p>Registers a javascript action on an element. When the action is performed, then the javascript will execute in place of the default behaviour.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to register the action on</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;actioned&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>clicked</code> to perform the action when the element is clicked</li>
        <li><code>right clicked</code> to perform the action when the element is right clicked, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>double clicked</code> to perform the action when the element is double clicked, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>submitted</code> to perform the action when the form element is submitted</li>
        <li><code>checked</code> (or <code>ticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to perform the action when the checkbox element is ticked</li>
        <li><code>unchecked</code> (or <code>unticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to perform the action when the checkbox element is unticked</li>
        <li><code>selected</code> to perform the action when a dropdown option is selected in the element</li>
        <li><code>deselected</code> to perform the action when a mutli-select dropdown option is deselected in the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>typed</code> to perform the action when text is typed into the element</li>
        <li><code>entered</code> to perform the action when text is entered into the element</li>
        <li><code>tabbed</code> to perform the action when the tab key is pressed in the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.17.1">v2.17.1</Link></li>
        <li><code>cleared</code> to perform the action when the text is cleared in the element</li>
        <li><code>moved to</code> to perform the action when the focus is moved to the element</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript|js&gt;</code> is <code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> , since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>)</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;script&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or function that will perform the action (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>The reference to the element will be provided to the javascript through an implicit object named <code>element</code>.</li>
        <li>For a one liner expression, no function, arrow declaration or <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>
          For a function, use either:
          <ul>
            <li><Link to="/docs/js-functions">Arrow syntax</Link> (preferred): <code>() =&gt; &#123; body &#125;</code> (Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.56.0">v3.56.0</Link>)</li>
            <li>Or anonymous function syntax (legacy): <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code></li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the submit button can be located by css ".submit"
      And the submit button can be clicked by js "element.click()"
     When I click the submit button
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-actioned-by-javascript">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.8.0">v1.8.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Download actions

<details id="i-download-to-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I download "<url>" to "<filepath>"
  ```
  <p>Downloads a resource from a URL to a file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;url&gt;</code> is URL to the resource to download</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> is the path of the file to download the resource to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
     When I download "https://example.com/file.pdf" to "output/download/file.pdf"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-download-to-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.58.0">v3.58.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-download-to-file-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I download "<url>" to <filepathRef file>
  ```
  <p>Downloads a resource from a URL to a referenced file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;url&gt;</code> is URL to the resource to download</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file to download the resource to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given my out file is "output/download/file.pdf"
     When I download "https://example.com/file.pdf" to my out file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-download-to-file-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.58.0">v3.58.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-download-current-url-to-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I download the current URL to "<filepath>"
  ```
  <p>Downloads the resource at the current URL to a file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> is the path of the file to download the resource to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
     When I navigate to "https://example.com/file.pdf"
      And I download the current URL to "output/download/file.pdf"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-download-current-url-to-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.58.0">v3.58.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-download-current-url-to-file-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I download the current URL to <filepathRef file>
  ```
  <p>Downloads a resource at the current URL to a referenced file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file to download the resource to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given my out file is "output/download/file.pdf"
     When I navigate to "https://example.com/file.pdf"
      And I download the current URL to my out file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-download-current-url-to-file-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.58.0">v3.58.0</Link></div>

</details>

#### File actions

<details id="i-attach-filepath-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I attach "<filepath>" as "<name>"
  ```
  or since v3.0.0
  ```gherkin
  I attach "<filepath>" as <name>
  ```

  <p>Attaches a local file to the Gwen report and assigns it a name. The link to the attachment in the report will have the given name.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the local file to attach</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> the name to assign to the file attachment</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
     When I attach "path/to/data.csv" as "data"
  ```
  Or since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.0.0">v3.0.0</Link>

  ```gherkin
     When I attach "path/to/data.csv" as data
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-attach-filepath-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.52.0">v2.52.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-attach-filepath">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I attach "<filepath>"
  ```


  <p>Attaches a local file to the Gwen report and assigns it the same name as the file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the local file to attach</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
     When I attach "path/to/data.csv"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-attach-filepath">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.0.0">v4.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-write-append-text-to-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> "<text>" to "<filepath>" file
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends text to a file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with the provided text</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append the provided text to existing content in file</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> the text to write or append to the file</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the local file to write or append the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
     When I write "automation" to "path/to/file.txt" file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-write-append-text-to-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.25.0">v3.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>


<details id="i-write-append-text-ref-to-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> <textRef> to "<filepath>" file
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends a text reference value to a file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with the provided text</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append the provided text to existing content in file</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to write or append to the file
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the local file to write or append the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {6}
     Given my content is
           """
           Automation and robotics
           for Gherkin
           """
     When I write my content to "path/to/file.txt" file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-write-append-text-ref-to-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.25.0">v3.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-write-append-new-line-to-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> new line to "<filepath>" file
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends a new line to a file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with a new line</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append a new line to existing content in file</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the local file to write or append the new line to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
     When I append new line to "path/to/file.txt" file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-write-append-new-line-to-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.25.0">v3.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-write-append-text-to-file-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> "<text>" to <filepathRef file>
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends text to a referenced file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with the provided text</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append the provided text to existing content in file</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> the text to write or append to the file</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file to write or append the provided text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
     Given my file is "path/to/file.txt"
      When I append "automation" to my file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-write-append-text-to-file-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.25.0">v3.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-write-append-text-ref-to-file-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> <textRef> to <filepathRef file>
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends a text reference value to a referenced file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with the provided text</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append the provided text to existing content in file</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to write or append to the file
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file to write or append the provided text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {7}
     Given my file is "path/to/file.txt"
       And my content is
           """
           Automation and robotics
           for Gherkin
           """
     When I write my content to my file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-write-append-text-ref-to-file-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.25.0">v3.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-write-append-new-line-to-file-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> new line to <filepathRef file>
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends a new line to a referenced file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with a new line</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append a new line to existing content in file</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file to write or append the new line to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
     Given my file is "path/to/file.txt"
      When I append new line to my file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-write-append-new-line-to-file-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.25.0">v3.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-log-record-to-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I log record to <resultsFileId> file
  ```

  <p>Logs a record to the results file having the given ID (if results is specifed in the format launch option only).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;resultsFileId&gt;</code> the ID of the <Link to="/docs/reports/csv#results-files">results file</Link> to log a record to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
     When I log record to my.results file
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-log-record-to-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.0.0">v4.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Sleeps and waits

<details id="i-wait-for-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait for <element>
  ```
  <p>Waits for an element to appear on a page for a default number of seconds before timing out. The default timeout period is equal to the configured gwen.web.wait.seconds setting value. The default timeout can be overridden using the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to wait for</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # Wait for a dynamically rendered input field 
    Given the dynamic input field can be located by tag "input"
     When I wait for the dynamic input field
     Then the dynamic input field should be displayed
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-for-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-for-element-text">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait for <element> text
  ```
  <p>Waits for the text of an element to appear on a page for a default number of seconds before timing out.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to wait for the text to appear</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # Wait for a dynamically displayed token
    Given the one time token can be located by javascript "$('.token').get(0)"
     When I wait for the one time token text
      And I capture the one time token
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-for-element-text">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-element-is-state">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until <element> is[ not] <state>
  ```
  <p>Waits for an element to transition to a given state. The default timeout period is equal to the configured gwen.web.wait.seconds setting value. The default timeout can be overridden using the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to wait for</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the state if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;state&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>displayed</code> to wait until the element is displayed</li>
        <li><code>hidden</code> to wait until the element is not displayed</li>
        <li><code>checked</code> (or <code>ticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to wait until a checkbox is ticked</li>
        <li><code>unchecked</code> (or <code>unticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to wait until a checkbox is not ticked</li>
        <li><code>enabled</code> to wait until the element is enabled</li>
        <li><code>disabled</code> to wait until the element is disabled</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
      And the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Get the milk" in the todo field
      And I wait until my todo list is displayed
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-element-is-state">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.25.0">v2.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-javascript">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until "<javascript>"
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly executes the given javascript expression or function until true is returned using no delay interval and default timeout period. The default timeout period is equal to the configured <code>gwen.web.wait.seconds</code> setting value. The default timeout can be overridden using the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;javascript&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or function that will return a boolean value (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>For a one liner expression, no function, arrow declaration or <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>
          For a function, use either:
          <ul>
            <li><Link to="/docs/js-functions">Arrow syntax</Link> (preferred): <code>() =&gt; &#123; body &#125;</code> (Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.56.0">v3.56.0</Link>)</li>
            <li>Or anonymous function syntax (legacy): <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code></li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
   Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
    When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
     And I wait until "!!$('h1')"
    Then the heading should be "Welcome to our Script Challenge"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-javascript">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-filepath-exists">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until "<filepath>" file[ not] exists
  ```
  <p>Waits until a file exists (or not). The default timeout period is equal to the configured gwen.web.wait.seconds setting value. The default timeout can be overridden using the @Timeout annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file</li>
    <li><code>not</code> to wait until the file does not exist (negation)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin
     Then I wait until "path/to/filename1.csv" file exists
      And I wait until "path/to/filename2.csv" file not exists
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-filepath-exists">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-filepath-does-not-exist">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until "<filepath>" file does not exist
  ```
  <p>Waits until a file does not exist. The default timeout period is equal to the configured gwen.web.wait.seconds setting value. The default timeout can be overridden using the @Timeout annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin
      And I wait until "path/to/filename2.csv" file does not exist
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-filepath-does-not-exist">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-filepathref-exists">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until <filepathRef file>[ not] exists
  ```
  <p>Waits until a file exists (or not). The default timeout period is equal to the configured gwen.web.wait.seconds setting value. The default timeout can be overridden using the @Timeout annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file</li>
    <li><code>not</code> to wait until the file does not exist (negation)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {2-3}
    Given my file is "path/to/filename.csv""
     Then I wait until my file exists
      And I wait until my file not exists
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-filepathref-exists">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-filepathref-does-not-exist">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until <filepathRef file> does not exist
  ```
  <p>Waits until a file does not exist. The default timeout period is equal to the configured gwen.web.wait.seconds setting value. The default timeout can be overridden using the @Timeout annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given my file is "path/to/filename.csv""
      And I wait until my file does not exist
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">

  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-filepath-empty">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until "<filepath>" file is[ not] empty
  ```
  <p>Waits until a file is empty. The default timeout period is equal to the configured gwen.web.wait.seconds setting value. The default timeout can be overridden using the @Timeout annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file</li>
    <li><code>not</code> to wait until the file is not empty (negation)</li>
  </ul>

     Then I wait until "path/to/filename1.csv" file is empty

<details id="i-wait-until-filepathref-empty">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until <filepathRef file> is[ not] empty
  ```
  <p>Waits until a file is empty. The default timeout period is equal to the configured gwen.web.wait.seconds setting value. The default timeout can be overridden using the @Timeout annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file</li>
    <li><code>not</code> to wait until the file is not empty (negation)</li>
  </ul>

<details id="i-wait-until-condition">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until <condition>
  ```
  <p>Waits until a condition is satisfied. The default timeout period is equal to the configured gwen.web.wait.seconds setting value. The default timeout can be overridden using the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;condition&gt;</code> is either:
      <ul>
        <li>
          Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.54.0">v3.54.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li>the name of any binding that will return <code>true</code> when the condition is satisfied or <code>false</code> when it is not</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
        <li>
          Or in prior versions
          <ul>
            <li>the name of a binding containing a javascript function or expression that will return <code>true</code> when the condition is satisfied or <code>false</code> when it is not</li>
            <li>the name of a binding containing a <code>true</code> or <code>false</code> value literal, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.50.0">v3.50.0</Link></li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
   Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
     And the heading is displayed is defined by javascript "!!$('h1')"
    When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
     And I wait until the heading is displayed
    Then the heading should be "Welcome to our Script Challenge"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-condition">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-for-alert-or-confirmation-popup">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait for the <alert|confirmation> popup
  ```
  <p>Waits for the alert/confirmation popup to appear on a page for a default number of seconds before timing out. The default timeout period is equal to the configured gwen.web.wait.seconds setting value. The default timeout can be overridden using the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to wait for</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
  Given the alert link can be located by id "alert"
   When I navigate to "https://www.selenium.dev/selenium/web/alerts.html"
    And I click the alert link
    And I wait for the alert popup
   Then the alert popup message should not be blank
  ```
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-for-alert-or-confirmation-popup">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.11.0">v4.11.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-duration-seconds">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait <duration> second[s]
  ```
  <p>Sleeps for the given number of seconds.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;duration&gt;</code> is the number of seconds to sleep</li>
    <li>Include trailing <code>s</code> when specifying a <code>&lt;duration&gt;</code> that is not 1, omit otherwise</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I wait for 5 seconds
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-duration-seconds">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### JS execution

<details id="i-execute-javascript">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I execute <javascript|js> "<script>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a JavaScript expression or function.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript|js&gt;</code> is <code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>)</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;script&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or function to execute (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>For a one liner expression, no function, arrow declaration or <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>
          For a function, use either:
          <ul>
            <li><Link to="/docs/js-functions">Arrow syntax</Link> (preferred): <code>() =&gt; &#123; body &#125;</code> (Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.56.0">v3.56.0</Link>)</li>
            <li>Or anonymous function syntax (legacy): <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code></li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I execute js "alert('Hello Gwen World')"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-execute-javascript">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.9.0">v2.9.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### System process execution

<details id="i-execute-system-process">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I execute system process "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a local system process or script.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the system process or script to execute</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I execute system process "echo 'Hello Gwen World'"
     And I execute system process "path/to/script.bat"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-execute-system-process">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-execute-system-process-delimited-by-delimiters">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I execute system process "<expression>" delimited by "<delimiters>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a delimited local system process or script.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> the delimited system process to execute
      <ul>
        <li>Delmiters are required for special cases such as when unbalanced quoted strings are passed as arguments (see example).</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;delmiters&gt;</code> is a regex pattern defining the delimiter(s) used in <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I execute system process "echo,"quoted text " and orphan quote"" delimited by ","
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-execute-system-process-delimited-by-delimiters">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-execute-a-unix-system-process">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I execute a unix system process "<expression>"
  ```
  or since v3.14.2
  ```gherkin
  I execute unix system process "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a local unix system process or shell script.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the system process or script to execute</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1,2}
    When I execute a unix system process "echo 'Hello Gwen World'"
     And I execute a unix system process "./path/to/script.sh"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-execute-a-unix-system-process">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-execute-a-unix-system-process-delimited-by-delimiters">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I execute unix system process "<expression>" delimited by "<delimiters>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a delimited local unix system process or script.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> the delimited system process to execute
      <ul>
        <li>Delmiters are required for special cases such as when unbalanced quoted strings are passed as arguments (see example).</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;delmiters&gt;</code> is a regex pattern defining the delimiter(s) used in <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I execute a unix system process "echo,"quoted text " and orphan quote"" delimited by ","
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-execute-a-unix-system-process-delimited-by-delimiters">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### SQL execution

<details id="name-is-defined-by-database-select-statement">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined in the <dbName> database by sql "<selectStmt>"
  ```
  
  <p>Associates the result of an SQL database query to the given name in the global scope. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the SQL query result to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;dbName&gt;</code> the name of the configured database to execute the query on</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selectStmt&gt;</code> is the SQL query that will return the value to assign (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>

  <p>Configuration</p>
  <ul>
    <li>The `GWEN_CLASSPATH` environment variable must be set to include a path to the JDBC driver JAR</li>
    <li>A <code>gwen.db.&lt;dbName&gt;.driver</code> setting must be set to the name of the JDBC driver implementation class</li>
    <li>A <code>gwen.db.&lt;dbName&gt;.url</code> setting must be set to the JDBC URL of the database</li>
  </ul>

  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code>, <code>@Lazy</code></Link> or <code>@Masked</code> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either of the above annotations, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
      <li><code>@Masked</code> masks the captured value to prevent it from being logged as clear text</li>
    </ul>
  </p>

  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1-4}
    Given the email address is defined in the feedback database by sql
          """
          select email from comments
          """
     Then the email address should be "some.person@example.com"
  ```

<Tabs
  groupId="setup"
  defaultValue="linux"
  values={[
    {label: 'Linux', value: 'linux'},
    {label: 'Windows', value: 'windows'},
  ]}>
  
<TabItem value="linux">

  Set GWEN_CLASSPATH variable in the environment to include the JDBC driver JAR

  ```shell
  export GWEN_CLASSPATH=/path-to-driver/mysql-connector-java-5.1.40-bin.jar
  ```

</TabItem>
<TabItem value="windows">

  Set GWEN_CLASSPATH variable in the environment to include the JDBC driver JAR

  ```shell
  set GWEN_CLASSPATH c:/path-to-driver/mysql-connector-java-5.1.40-bin.jar
  ```

</TabItem>
</Tabs>

  Configure the database in your settings. In this example, <code>&lt;dbName&gt;</code>=feedback

  ```properties
  gwen.db.feedback.driver = com.mysql.jdbc.Driver
  gwen.db.feedback.url = jdbc:mysql://localhost/feedback?user=myUser&amp;password=myPassword&amp;
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-database-select-statement">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2017/02/13/sql-data-bindings-for-gwen">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.10.0">v2.10.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-update-database-by-sql-update-statement">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I update the <dbName> database by sql "<updateStmt>"
  ```
  <p>Executes an SQL udpate statement on a configured database.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dbName&gt;</code> the name of the configured database to run the update statement on</li>
    <li><code>&lt;updateStmt&gt;</code> is the SQL update statement to execute (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>

  <p>Returns</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dbName&gt; rows affected</code> = the number of rows affected by the update</li>
  </ul>

  <p>Configuration</p>
  <ul>
    <li>The `GWEN_CLASSPATH` environment variable must be set to include a path to the JDBC driver JAR</li>
    <li>A <code>gwen.db.&lt;dbName&gt;.driver</code> setting must be set to the name of the JDBC driver implementation class</li>
    <li>A <code>gwen.db.&lt;dbName&gt;.url</code> setting must be set to the JDBC URL of the database</li>
  </ul>

  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I update the feedback database by sql
         """
         update comments set email='new@example.com' where email='old@example.com'
         """
    Then feedback rows affected should be "1"
  ```

  <Tabs
  groupId="setup"
  defaultValue="linux"
  values={[
    {label: 'Linux', value: 'linux'},
    {label: 'Windows', value: 'windows'},
  ]}>

<TabItem value="linux">

  Set GWEN_CLASSPATH variable in the environment to include the JDBC driver JAR

  ```shell
  export GWEN_CLASSPATH=/path-to-driver/mysql-connector-java-5.1.40-bin.jar
  ```

</TabItem>
<TabItem value="windows">

  Set GWEN_CLASSPATH variable in the environment to include the JDBC driver JAR

  ```shell
  set GWEN_CLASSPATH c:/path-to-driver/mysql-connector-java-5.1.40-bin.jar
  ```

</TabItem>
</Tabs>

  Configure the database in your settings. In this example, <code>&lt;dbName&gt;</code>=feedback

  ```properties
  gwen.db.feedback.driver = com.mysql.jdbc.Driver
  gwen.db.feedback.url = jdbc:mysql://localhost/feedback?user=myUser&amp;password=myPassword&amp;
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-update-database-by-sql-update-statement">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2017/02/13/sql-data-bindings-for-gwen">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

### Assertions

#### Text asserts

<details id="text-ref-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] be <blank|empty>
  ```

  <p>Checks whether or not the text reference matches a blank or empty string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>

  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] be <blank|empty>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <textRef> should[ not] be blank
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <textRef> should[ not] be blank
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to check
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {6}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Get the milk" in the todo field
      And I capture my todo list as current items
     Then current items should not be empty
  ```

  Trimming (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#text-ref-should-match-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.26.0">v3.26.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="text-ref-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```

  <p>Checks whether or not the text reference matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>

  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <textRef> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <textRef> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to check
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {6}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Get the milk" in the todo field
      And I capture my todo list as current items
     Then current items should contain "Get the milk"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#text-ref-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="text-ref-should-match-expression-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the value of a variable or setting matches a referenced expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>

  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <textRef> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <textRef> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;variable&gt;</code> is the name of the variable or setting to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an expression value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {7}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
      And my item is "Feed the cat"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter my item in the todo field
      And I capture my todo list as current items
     Then current items should contain my item
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#text-ref-should-match-expression-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="text-ref-should-be-similar-to-text">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to "<text>"
  ```

  <p>Compares a text reference with a text value for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to "<text>"  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <textRef> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to "<text>"
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <textRef> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to "<text>"
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing a text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>match</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>be less than</code> for less than match</li>
        <li><code>be at most</code> for less than or equal to match</li>
        <li><code>be more than</code> for greater than match</li>
        <li><code>be at least</code> for greater than or equal to match</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> is the text to compare <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> against</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  The calculated similarity score is implicity bound to the <code>similarity score</code> attribute in the global scope.
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {2-7}
    Given the phrase is "Hello world!"
     Then the phrase should be more than 90% similar to "Hello world"
      And @IgnoreCase the phrase should be at least 90% similar to "hello world"
      And the phrase should be 94.12% similar to "Hello world"
      And @IgnoreCase the phrase should be 94.12% similar to "hello world"
      And the phrase should be 82.35% similar to "hello world"
      And the phrase should not be less than 90% similar to "Hello world"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#text-ref-should-be-similar-to-text">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.0">v3.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="text-ref-1-should-be-similar-to-text-ref-2">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <textRef1> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to <textRef2>
  ```

  <p>Compares a text reference with another for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef1> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to <textRef2>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <textRef1> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to <textRef2>
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <textRef1> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to <textRef2>
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef1&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the first text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>match</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>be less than</code> for less than match</li>
        <li><code>be at most</code> for less than or equal to match</li>
        <li><code>be more than</code> for greater than match</li>
        <li><code>be at least</code> for greater than or equal to match</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;percentage&gt;</code> is a percentage number between 0 and 100 (internally rounded to 2 decimal places)</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef2&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the second text reference to compare <code>&lt;textRef1&gt;</code> against
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  The calculated similarity score is implicity bound to the <code>similarity score</code> attribute in the global scope.
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {4-9}
    Given phrase 1 is "Hello world!"
      And phrase 2 is "Hello world"
      And phrase 3 is "hello world"
     Then phrase 1 should be more than 90% similar to phrase 2
      And @IgnoreCase phrase 1 should be at least 90% similar to phrase 2
      And phrase 1 should be 94.12% similar to phrase 2
      And @IgnoreCase phrase 1 should be 94.12% similar to phrase 3
      And phrase 1 should be 82.35% similar to phrase 3
      And phrase 1 should not be less than 90% similar to phrase 2
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#text-ref-1-should-be-similar-to-text-ref-2">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.0">v3.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### File asserts

<details id="filepath-should-exist">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  "<filepath>" file should[ not] exist
  ```
  <p>Asserts that a file should exist (or not).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code>to check that the file does not exist (negation)</li>
  </ul>
  
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
     Then "path/to/existing.txt" file should exist
      And "path/to/missing.txt" file should not exist
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#filepath-should-exist">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="filepathref-should-exist">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <filepathRef file> should[ not] exist
  ```
  <p>Asserts that a file should exist (or not).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code>to check that the file does not exist (negation)</li>
  </ul>
  
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3-4}
    Given my existing file is "path/to/existing.txt"
      And my missing file is "path/to/missing.txt"
     Then my existing file should exist
     Then my missing file should not exist
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#filepathref-should-exist">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="filepath-should-be-empty">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  "<filepath>" file should[ not] be empty
  ```
  <p>Asserts that a file should be empty (or not).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code>to check that the file is not empty (negation)</li>
  </ul>
  
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
     Then "path/to/empty.txt" file should be empty
      And "path/to/populated.txt" file should not be empty
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#filepath-should-be-empty">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="filepathref-should-be-empty">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <filepathRef file> should[ not] be empty
  ```
  <p>Asserts that a file should be empty (or not).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code>to check that the file is not empty (negation)</li>
