#### XML asserts

<details id="xml-ref-at-xpath-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not] be <blank|empty>
  ```
  
  <p>Extracts text from the referenced XML value using the given XPath and checks whether or not it matches a blank or empty string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not] be blank
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not] be blank
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;xmlRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the XML source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an XML text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>path</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the xml is "<result><status>passed</status></result>"
     Then the xml at xpath "//result/status" should not be blank
  ```

  Trimming (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#xml-ref-at-xpath-should-match-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.26.0">v3.26.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="xml-ref-at-xpath-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Extracts text from the referenced XML value using the given XPath and checks that it matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not] <match> "<expression>"  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;xmlRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the XML source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an XML text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>path</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the xml is "<result><status>passed</status></result>"
     Then the xml at xpath "//result/status" should be "passed"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#xml-ref-at-xpath-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.6.0">v2.6.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### JSON asserts

<details id="json-ref-at-json-path-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <jsonRef> at json path "<path>" should[ not] be <blank|empty>
  ```
  
  <p>Extracts text from the referenced JSON value using the given JSON path and checks whether or not it matches a blank or empty string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <jsonRef> at json path "<path>" should[ not] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <jsonRef> at json path "<path>" should[ not] be blank
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <jsonRef> at json path "<path>" should[ not] be blank
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;jsonRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the JSON source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a JSON text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>path</code> is the <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON path</Link> selector expression</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
      Given the json is "{ "status": "passed" }"
       Then the json at json path "$.status" should not be blank
  ```

  Trimming (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#json-ref-at-json-path-should-match-blank">Link</Link></div>

  </div>
</details>

<details id="json-ref-at-json-path-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <jsonRef> at json path "<path>" should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```

  </summary>

  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>

        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a JSON text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>path</code> is the <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON path</Link> selector expression</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>

#### URL asserts

<details id="the-current-url-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] be <blank|empty>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the current browser URL matches a blank or empty string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') the current URL should[ not] be blank
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') the current URL should[ not] be blank
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
    Then the current URL should not be blank
  ```

  Trimming (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-current-url-should-match-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.26.0">v3.26.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="the-current-url-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the current browser URL matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>

  ```gherkin

  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') the current URL should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2,3}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
    Then the current URL should contain "todomvc.com"
     And the current URL should not contain "other.com"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-current-url-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="the-current-url-should-match-expression-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the current URL in the browser matches a referenced expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') the current URL should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') the current URL should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an expression value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4,5}
    Given my domain is "todomvc.com"
      And some other domain is "someother.com"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     Then the current URL should contain my domain
      And the current URL should not contain some other domain
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-current-url-should-match-expression-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Page title asserts

<details id="the-page-title-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the page title should[ not] be <blank|empty>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the title of the current page matches a blank or empty string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the page title should[ not] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') the page title should[ not] be blank
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') the page title should[ not] be blank
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
    Then the page title should not be blank
  ```

  Trimming (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
  </ul>

<details id="the-page-title-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the page title should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the title of the current page in the browser matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>



  ```gherkin

  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>

      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>

        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON path</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>

      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>


  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON path</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>

      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>

      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>

#### Element asserts

<details id="element-should-be-state">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] be <state>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not an element is in a given state.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] be <state>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <element> should[ not] be <state>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <element> should[ not] be <state>
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the state if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;state&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>displayed</code> to check if the element is displayed</li>
        <li><code>hidden</code> to check if the element is not displayed</li>
        <li><code>checked</code> (or <code>ticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to check if a checkbox is ticked</li>
        <li><code>unchecked</code> (or <code>unticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to check if a checkbox is not ticked</li>
        <li><code>enabled</code> to check if the element is enabled</li>
        <li><code>disabled</code> to check if the element is disabled</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     Then my todo list should be empty
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-should-be-state">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the text value of an element matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <element> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <element> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Get the milk" in the todo field
     Then my todo list should contain "Get the milk"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-should-match-expression-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  <p>Checks whether or not the text value of an element matches a referenced expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <element> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <element> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an expression value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {6}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
      And my item is "Feed the cat"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter my item in the todo field
     Then my todo list should contain my item
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-should-match-expression-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Dropdown asserts

<details id="drodown-text-or-value-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] be <blank|empty>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not a dropdown selection matches a blank or empty string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] be blank
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] be blank
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the dropdown element to check</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;text|value&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to check the displayed text of the selection</li>
        <li><code>value</code> to check the option value of the selection</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select the 2nd option in the age dropdown
     Then the age dropdown value should not be blank
  ```

  Trimming (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#drodown-text-or-value-should-match-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.26.0">v3.26.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="drodown-text-or-value-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not a dropdown selection matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the dropdown element to check</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;text|value&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to check the displayed text of the selection</li>
        <li><code>value</code> to check the option value of the selection</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select the 2nd option in the age dropdown
     Then the age dropdown value should be "18"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#drodown-text-or-value-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="drodown-text-or-value-should-match-expression-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not a dropdown selection matches a referenced expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the dropdown element to check</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;text|value&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to check the displayed text of the selection</li>
        <li><code>value</code> to check the option value of the selection</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an expression value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
      And my age is "18"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select the 2nd option in the age dropdown
     Then the age dropdown value should be my age
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#drodown-text-or-value-should-match-expression-ref">Link</Link></div>

#### Browser asserts

<details id="i-should-have-1-open-browser">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I should have 1 open browser
  ```
  <p>Checks that only one browser session is currently open. Reports an assertion error if not.</p>
  </summary>

  <p>

  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  I should have 1 open browser  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```
  
  </p>

  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
   Given I have no open browser
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
    Then I should have 1 open browser
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-should-have-1-open-browser">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.41.0">v2.41.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-should-have-count-open-browsers">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I should have <count> open browsers
  ```
  <p>Checks that a given number of browsers are currently open. Reports an assertion error if not.</p>
  </summary>

  <p>

  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  I should have <count> open browsers  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>

  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>count</code> the expected number of open browsers</li>
  </ul>

  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
   Given I have no open browser
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
     And I start a browser for Vue
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/vue"
    Then I should have 2 open browsers
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-should-have-count-open-browsers">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.41.0">v2.41.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Alert and Popup asserts

<details id="the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] be <blank|empty>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the message in the alert or confirmation popup box matches a blank or empty string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] be blank
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] be blank
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the alert link can be located by id "alert"
     When I navigate to "https://www.selenium.dev/selenium/web/alerts.html"
      And I click the alert link
     Then the alert popup message should not be blank
  ```

  Trimming (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.26.0">v3.26.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the message in the alert or confirmation popup box matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>


  </p>

  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>


  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

