  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the alert link can be located by id "alert"
     When I navigate to "https://www.selenium.dev/selenium/web/alerts.html"
      And I click the alert link
     Then the alert popup message should be "cheese"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.24.0">v2.24.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-expression-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the message in the alert or confirmation popup box matches a referenced expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an expression value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the confirmation link can be located by id "prompt-with-default"
      And the expected message is "Enter something"
     When I navigate to "https://www.selenium.dev/selenium/web/alerts.html"
      And I click the confirmation link
     Then the confirmation popup message should be the expected message
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-expression-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.24.0">v2.24.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-should-be-displayed">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup should[ not] be displayed
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the alert/comnfirmation popup should be displayed or not. Reports an assertion error if the assertion fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message:</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup should[ not] be displayed  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout:</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') the <alert|confirmation> popup should[ not] be displayed
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout:</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') the <alert|confirmation> popup should[ not] be displayed
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;alert|confirmation&gt;</code> is either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>alert</code> for an alert box with an OK button</li>
        <li><code>confirmation</code> for a confirmation box with OK and Cancel buttons</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the assertion if included (should not be displayed)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the confirmation link can be located by id "prompt-with-default"
     When I navigate to "https://www.selenium.dev/selenium/web/alerts.html"
      And I click the confirmation link
     Then the confirmation popup should be displayed
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-should-be-displayed">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.11.0">v4.11.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Existential asserts

<details id="name-should-be-absent">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be absent
  ```

  <p>Checks that a named binding is absent from the current scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be absent  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <name> should be absent
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <name> should be absent
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the binding to check</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    Then this should be absent
  ```
  
  or equivalently (as of v3.29.0)

  ```gherkin
    Then that should not be defined
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-should-be-absent">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.6.0">v2.6.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-should-be-defined">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> should[ not] be defined
  ```

  <p>Checks whether or not a named binding exists in the current scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>With custom assertion error message:</p>

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be defined  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Without any timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('0s') <name> should be defined
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>With custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  @Timeout('10s') <name> should be defined
  ```

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the binding to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the check (for absence/non existence)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  To check for the presence of a binding
  
  ```gherkin
    Then this should be defined
  ```

  To check for the absence of a binding
  
  ```gherkin
    Then that should not be defined
  ```

  or equivalently

  ```gherkin
    Then that should be absent
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-should-be-defined">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.29.0">v3.29.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Cumulative asserts

<details id="there-should-be-no-accumulated-errors">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  there should be no accumulated errors
  ```

  <p>Checks that no errors were raised prior to this been called and raises all accumulated error messages (if any) in one assertion error.</p>
  </summary>

  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4} showLineNumbers
    Then @Soft x should not be blank
     And @Soft y should be "1"
     And @Soft z should be true
     And there should be no accumulated errors
  ```

  Line 4 will pass if all the preceeding assertions pass. If however, the assertions on line 1 and 3 fail (and the one on line 2 passes), then it will raise an assertion error containing the two messages as follows:

  ```
  2 errors:
  (1) x should not be blank
  (2) z should be true but got false
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#there-should-be-no-accumulated-errors">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="/docs/assertions#cumulative-assertions">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.61.0">v3.61.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-reset-accumulated-errors">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I reset accumulated errors
  ```

  <p>Resets (clears) any previously accumulated errors.</p>
  </summary>

  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1} showLineNumbers
    When I reset accumulated errors
    Then @Soft x should not be blank
     And @Soft y should be "1"
     And @Soft z should be true
     And there should be no accumulated errors
  ```

  Line 1 will clear any previously accumulated errors from the currently executing context.

  So only the messages of all failed assertions leading up to line 4 will be included.

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-reset-accumulated-errors">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="/docs/assertions#cumulative-assertions">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.61.0">v3.61.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Data asserts

<details id="name-should-be-unique-in-the-filepath-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be unique in the "<filepath>" file
  ```
  <p>Checks that the current value of a field (or aggregation of fields) is unique in a CSV or JSON input file</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code>the name of the field (or comma separated fields aggregation) to check</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the CSV or JSON file</li>
  </ul>

  <p>Examples</p>

  ##### CSV Check

  Given the CSV file: resources/StateCodes.csv

  ```csv
  Code,Name
  ACT,Australian Capital Territory
  NSW,New South Wales
  NT,Northern Territory
  QLD,Queensland
  SA,South Australia
  TAS,Tasmania
  VIC,Victoria
  WA,Western Australia
  ```

  The following will check that all values in the <code>Name</code> column are unique:

  ```gherkin {1}
    Then Name should be unique in the "resources/StateCodes.csv" file
  ```

  ##### JSON Check

  Given the JSON file: resources/StateCodes.json

  ```json
  [
    { "Code": "ACT", "Name": "Australian Capital Territory" },
    { "Code": "NSW", "Name": "New South Wales" },
    { "Code": "NT",  "Name": "Northern Territory" },
    { "Code": "QLD", "Name": "Queensland" },
    { "Code": "SA",  "Name": "South Australia" },
    { "Code": "TAS", "Name": "Tasmania" },
    { "Code": "VIC", "Name": "Victoria" },
    { "Code": "WA",  "Name": "Western Australia" }
  ]
  ```

  The following will check that all <code>Name</code> properties are unique:

  ```gherkin {1}
    Then Name should be unique in the "resources/StateCodes.json" file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-should-be-unique-in-the-filepath-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.12.0">v4.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-should-be-unique-in-the-filepath-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be unique in <filepathRef file>
  ```
  <p>Checks that the current value of a field (or aggregation of fields) is unique in a CSV or JSON input file</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code>the name of the field (or comma separated fields aggregation) to check</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the CSV or JSON file</li>
  </ul>

  The data value contained in the first record that satisifes the given predicate will be bound to the global scope. Otherwise if no records match, then no value will be bound.

  <p>Examples</p>

  ##### CSV Check

  Given the CSV file: resources/StateCodes.csv

  ```csv
  Code,Name
  ACT,Australian Capital Territory
  NSW,New South Wales
  NT,Northern Territory
  QLD,Queensland
  SA,South Australia
  TAS,Tasmania
  VIC,Victoria
  WA,Western Australia
  ```

  The following will check that all values in the <code>Name</code> column are unique:

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the mapping file is "resources/StateCodes.csv"
     Then Name should be unique in the mapping file
  ```

  ##### JSON Check

  Given the JSON file: resources/StateCodes.json

  ```json
  [
    { "Code": "ACT", "Name": "Australian Capital Territory" },
    { "Code": "NSW", "Name": "New South Wales" },
    { "Code": "NT",  "Name": "Northern Territory" },
    { "Code": "QLD", "Name": "Queensland" },
    { "Code": "SA",  "Name": "South Australia" },
    { "Code": "TAS", "Name": "Tasmania" },
    { "Code": "VIC", "Name": "Victoria" },
    { "Code": "WA",  "Name": "Western Australia" }
  ]
  ```

  The following will check that all <code>Name</code> properties are unique:

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given the mapping file is "resources/StateCodes.json"
     Then Name should be unique in the mapping file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-should-be-unique-in-the-filepath-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.12.0">v4.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

### Control structures

#### ForEach

> Since [v3.48.0](https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.47.0), the following implicit attributes are available to <code>&lt;step&gt;</code>s:
> <ul>
>  <li><code>gwen.iteration.number</code> = current iteration starting at 1</li>
>  <li><code>gwen.iteration.index</code> = current iteration starting at 0</li>
> </ul>

<details id="step-for-each-element-located-by-selector-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> for each <element> located by <selector> "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a step for each element in a list of elements in the current scope with a default lookup timeout that can be overridden with the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute for each element</li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name that will be assigned to the current element occurrence (element is accessible in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code> by this name)</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression returning one or many elements</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {6}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And the active count can be located by css ".todo-count"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I enter "Feed the cat" in the todo field
      And I tick todo item for each todo item located by css ".todo-list .toggle"
     Then the active count should contain "0"
  ```

  With explicit timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {6}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And the active count can be located by css ".todo-count"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I enter "Feed the cat" in the todo field
      And @Timeout('10s') I tick todo item for each todo item located by css ".todo-list .toggle"
     Then the active count should contain "0"
  ```

  Without any timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {6}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And the active count can be located by css ".todo-count"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I enter "Feed the cat" in the todo field
      And @Timeout('0s') I tick todo item for each todo item located by css ".todo-list .toggle"
     Then the active count should contain "0"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-for-each-element-located-by-selector-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-for-each-element-located-by-selector-expression-in-container">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> for each <element> located by <selector> "<expression>" in <containerElement>
  ```
  <p>Executes a step for each element in a list of elements in a container element in the current scope with a default lookup timeout that can be overridden with the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute for each element</li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name that will be assigned to the current element occurrence (element is accessible in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code> by this name)</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression returning one or many elements</li>
    <li><code>&lt;containerElement&gt;</code> is the name assigned to the container element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {7}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And the todo list can be located by class "todo-list"
      And the active count can be located by css ".todo-count"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I enter "Feed the cat" in the todo field
      And I tick todo item for each todo item located by class "toggle" in the todo list
     Then the active count should contain "0"
  ```

  With explicit timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

 ```gherkin {7}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And the todo list can be located by class "todo-list"
      And the active count can be located by css ".todo-count"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I enter "Feed the cat" in the todo field
      And @Timeout('10s') I tick todo item for each todo item located by class "toggle" in the todo list
     Then the active count should contain "0"
  ```

  Without any timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {7}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And the todo list can be located by class "todo-list"
      And the active count can be located by css ".todo-count"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I enter "Feed the cat" in the todo field
      And @Timeout('0s') I tick todo item for each todo item located by class "toggle" in the todo list
     Then the active count should contain "0"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-for-each-element-located-by-selector-expression-in-container">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-for-each-element-in-elements">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> for each <element> in <elements>
  ```
  <p>Executes a step for each element in a list of elements in the current scope with a default lookup timeout that can be overridden with the `@Timeout` annotation.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute for each element</li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name that will be assigned to the current element occurrence (element is accessible in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code> by this name)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;elements&gt;</code> is the name of the locator binding returning multiple elements</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {7}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And the active count can be located by css ".todo-count"
      And all todo items can be located by css ".todo-list .toggle"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I enter "Feed the cat" in the todo field
      And I tick todo item for each todo item in all todo items
     Then the active count should contain "0"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-for-each-element-in-elements">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-for-each-data-record">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> for each data record
  ```
  <p>Executes a step for each record in a data table.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute for each record</li>
    <li>Each field in a record can be accessed in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code> using the field's associated header name</li>
    <li>
      The following implicit bindings are available in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code>:
      <ul>
        <li><code>gwen.table.record.number</code> is the current record number (starting at 1)</li>
        <li><code>gwen.table.record.index</code> is the record index (starting at 0), since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.30.1">v2.30.1</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>
  
  <em>Feature</em>

  ```gherkin
    Scenario: my scenario
      Given I have the following active items
            | Item         |
            | Walk the dog |
            | Get the milk |
            | Feed the cat |
  ```

  <em>Meta</em>

  ```gherkin {7}
    @StepDef
    @DataTable
    Scenario: I have the following active items
      Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
        And the active count can be located by css ".todo-count"
       When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
        And I enter Item in the todo field for each data record
       Then the active count should contain "3"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-for-each-data-record">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="for-each-entry-in-text-ref-delimited-by">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> for each <entry> in <textRef> delimited by "<delimiter>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a step for each delimited text entry.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute for each delimited entry</li>
    <li><code>&lt;entry&gt;</code> is the name that will be assigned to the current entry occurrence (entry is accessible in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code> by this name)</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the delimitted values
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a delmited list of values, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;delimiter&gt;</code> the delimiter used in <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> to separate each value</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And the active count can be located by css ".todo-count"
      And my items is "Walk the dog, Feed the cat, Get the milk"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter item in the todo field for each item in my items delimited by ","
     Then the active count should contain "3"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#for-each-entry-in-text-ref-delimited-by">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="for-each-entry-in-json-array">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> for each <entry> in <arrayRef> array"
  ```
  <p>Executes a step for each text entry in a JSON array.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute for each entry</li>
    <li><code>&lt;entry&gt;</code> is the name that will be assigned to the current entry occurrence (entry is accessible in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code> by this name)</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;arrayRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the string repersentation of the JSON array
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a JSON array string, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {12}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And the active count can be located by css ".todo-count"
      And my items is
          """
          [ 
            "Walk the dog", 
            "Feed the cat", 
            "Get the milk" 
          ]
          """
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react/dist"
      And I enter item in the todo field for each item in my items array
     Then the active count should contain "3"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#for-each-entry-in-json-array">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="/docs/data-feeds#looping-nested-arrays">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.66.0">v3.66.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Until/While

> Since [v3.48.0](https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.47.0), the following implicit attributes are available to <code>&lt;step&gt;</code>s:
> <ul>
>  <li><code>gwen.iteration.number</code> = current iteration starting at 1</li>
>  <li><code>gwen.iteration.index</code> = current iteration starting at 0</li>
> </ul>


<details id="step-until-or-while-condition">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <until|while> <condition>
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while a condition is satisfied using a default delay and timeout period. The default delay between iterations is one tenth of the configured <code>gwen.web.wait.seconds</code> setting (or 1 second if not set). The default timeout period is 30 times the delay. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the `@Delay` and `@Timeout` annotations.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute in each iteration</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;until|while&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>until</code> to repeat until the condition is satisfied</li>
        <li><code>while</code> to repeat while the condition is satisfied</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;condition&gt;</code> is either:
      <ul>
        <li>
          Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.54.0">v3.54.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li>the name of any binding that will return <code>true</code> when the condition is satisfied or <code>false</code> when it is not</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
        <li>
          Or in prior versions
          <ul>
            <li>the name of a binding containing a javascript function or expression that will return <code>true</code> when the condition is satisfied or <code>false</code> when it is not</li>
            <li>the name of a binding containing a <code>true</code> or <code>false</code> value literal, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.50.0">v3.50.0</Link></li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      The following implicit binding is available in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code>:
      <ul>
        <li><code>iteration number</code> (or <code>gwen.iteration.number</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.52.0">v2.52.0</Link>) is the current iteration number (starting at 1)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {13}
      Given the search field can be located by name "q"
        And the next page link can be located by id "pnnext"
        And topic is "what is gwen"
        And topic link can be located by partial link text "${topic}"
        And topic not found is defined by js
            """
            [...document.querySelectorAll("a")]
              .filter(a => a.textContent.includes('${topic}'))
              .length == 0
            """
       When I navigate to "https://google.com"
        And I enter "gwen interpreter" in the search field
        And I click the next page link while topic not found
        And I click topic link
       Then the page title should contain "${topic}"
  ```

  With explicit delay and timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {13}
      Given the search field can be located by name "q"
        And the next page link can be located by id "pnnext"
        And topic is "what is gwen"
        And topic link can be located by partial link text "${topic}"
        And topic not found is defined by js
            """
            [...document.querySelectorAll("a")]
              .filter(a => a.textContent.includes('${topic}'))
              .length == 0
            """
       When I navigate to "https://google.com"
        And I enter "gwen interpreter" in the search field
        And @Delay('10s') @Timeout('1m') I click the next page link while topic not found
        And I click topic link
       Then the page title should contain "${topic}"
  ```

  With no delay or timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

  ```gherkin {13}
      Given the search field can be located by name "q"
        And the next page link can be located by id "pnnext"
        And topic is "what is gwen"
        And topic link can be located by partial link text "${topic}"
        And topic not found is defined by js
            """
            [...document.querySelectorAll("a")]
              .filter(a => a.textContent.includes('${topic}'))
              .length == 0
            """
       When I navigate to "https://google.com"
        And I enter "gwen interpreter" in the search field
        And @Delay('0s') @Timeout('0s') I click the next page link while topic not found
        And I click topic link
       Then the page title should contain "${topic}"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-until-or-while-condition">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-until-or-while-element-state">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <until|while> <element> is[ not] <state>
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while an element is in a given state using a 1 second delay interval and 1 minute timeout period. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the `@Delay` and `@Timeout` annotations.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute in each iteration</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;until|while&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>until</code> to repeat until the condition is satisfied</li>
        <li><code>while</code> to repeat while the condition is satisfied</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to check the state of</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the state if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;state&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>displayed</code> to execute the step until or while the element is displayed</li>
        <li><code>hidden</code> to execute the step until or while the element is not displayed</li>
        <li><code>checked</code> or <code>ticked</code> to execute the step until or while a checkbox is ticked</li>
        <li><code>unchecked</code> or <code>unticked</code> to execute the step until or while a checkbox is not ticked</li>
        <li><code>enabled</code> to execute the step until or while the element is enabled</li>
        <li><code>disabled</code> to execute the step until or while the element is disabled</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>
      The following implicit binding is available in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code>:
      <ul>
        <li><code>iteration number</code> (or <code>gwen.iteration.number</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.52.0">v2.52.0</Link>) is the current iteration number (starting at 1)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
      Given the search field can be located by name "q"
        And the next page link can be located by id "pnnext"
       When I navigate to "https://google.com"
        And I enter "gwen interpreter" in the search field
        And I click the next page link while the next page link is displayed
       Then the next page link should not be displayed
  ```

  With explicit delay and timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

   ```gherkin {5}
      Given the search field can be located by name "q"
        And the next page link can be located by id "pnnext"
       When I navigate to "https://google.com"
        And I enter "gwen interpreter" in the search field
        And @Delay('5s') @Timeout('40s') I click the next page link while the next page link is displayed
       Then the next page link should not be displayed
  ```

  With no delay or timeout since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.73.0">v3.73.0</Link>

   ```gherkin {5}
      Given the search field can be located by name "q"
        And the next page link can be located by id "pnnext"
       When I navigate to "https://google.com"
        And I enter "gwen interpreter" in the search field
        And @Delay('0s') @Timeout('0s') I click the next page link while the next page link is displayed
       Then the next page link should not be displayed
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-until-or-while-element-state">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.44.0">v3.44.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-until-or-while-defined">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <until|while> <name> is[ not] defined
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while an attribute is defined (or not) using a 1 second delay interval and 1 minute timeout period. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the `@Delay` and `@Timeout` annotations.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute in each iteration</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;until|while&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>until</code> to repeat until the attribute is defined (or not)</li>
        <li><code>while</code> to repeat while the attribute is defined (or not)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the attribute to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> include to execute step until or while attribute is not defined</li>
    <li>
      The following implicit binding is available in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code>:
      <ul>
        <li><code>iteration number</code> (or <code>gwen.iteration.number</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.52.0">v2.52.0</Link>) is the current iteration number (starting at 1)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-until-or-while-defined">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.57.0">v3.57.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-until-or-while-filepath-exists">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <until|while> "<filepath>" file[ not] exists
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while a file exists (or not) using a 1 second delay interval and 1 minute timeout period. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the `@Delay` and `@Timeout` annotations.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute in each iteration</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;until|while&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>until</code> to repeat until the attribute is defined (or not)</li>
        <li><code>while</code> to repeat while the attribute is defined (or not)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code>to wait until the file does not exist (negation)</li>
    <li>
      The following implicit binding is available in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code>:
      <ul>
        <li><code>iteration number</code> (or <code>gwen.iteration.number</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.52.0">v2.52.0</Link>) is the current iteration number (starting at 1)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-until-or-while-filepath-exists">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-until-or-while-filepath-does-not-exist">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <until|while> "<filepath>" file does not exist
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while a file does not exist using a 1 second delay interval and 1 minute timeout period. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the `@Delay` and `@Timeout` annotations.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute in each iteration</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;until|while&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>until</code> to repeat until the attribute is defined (or not)</li>
        <li><code>while</code> to repeat while the attribute is defined (or not)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file to check</li>
    <li>
      The following implicit binding is available in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code>:
      <ul>
        <li><code>iteration number</code> (or <code>gwen.iteration.number</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.52.0">v2.52.0</Link>) is the current iteration number (starting at 1)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-until-or-while-filepath-does-not-exist">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>


<details id="step-until-or-while-filepath-empty">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <until|while> "<filepath>" file is[ not] empty
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while a file is empty (or not) using a 1 second delay interval and 1 minute timeout period. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the `@Delay` and `@Timeout` annotations.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute in each iteration</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;until|while&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>until</code> to repeat until the attribute is defined (or not)</li>
        <li><code>while</code> to repeat while the attribute is defined (or not)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code>to wait until the file is not empty (negation)</li>
    <li>
      The following implicit binding is available in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code>:
      <ul>
        <li><code>iteration number</code> (or <code>gwen.iteration.number</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.52.0">v2.52.0</Link>) is the current iteration number (starting at 1)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-until-or-while-filepath-empty">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-until-or-while-filepathref-exists">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <until|while> <filepathRef file>[ not] exists
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while a file exists (or not) using a 1 second delay interval and 1 minute timeout period. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the `@Delay` and `@Timeout` annotations.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to execute in each iteration</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;until|while&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>until</code> to repeat until the attribute is defined (or not)</li>
        <li><code>while</code> to repeat while the attribute is defined (or not)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code>to wait until the file does not exist (negation)</li>
    <li>
      The following implicit binding is available in <code>&lt;step&gt;</code>:
      <ul>
        <li><code>iteration number</code> (or <code>gwen.iteration.number</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.52.0">v2.52.0</Link>) is the current iteration number (starting at 1)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-until-or-while-filepathref-exists">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-until-or-while-filepathref-empty">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <until|while> <filepathRef file> is[ not] empty
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while a file is empty (or not) using a 1 second delay interval and 1 minute timeout period. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the `@Delay` and `@Timeout` annotations.</p>

        <li><code>while</code> to repeat while the attribute is defined (or not)</li>
      </ul>

<details id="step-until-or-while-binding-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <while|until> <name> is[ not] <blank|empty>
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while an element or attribute is bound to a blank or empty value (or not) using a 1 second delay interval and 1 minute timeout period. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the @Delay and @Timeout annotations.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to repeatedly execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the element or attribute to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> to negate the condition</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
   Given the state code can be located by name "state"
    When I navigate to "https://example.com"
     And I refresh the current page while the state code is blank
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-until-or-while-binding-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.1.0">v4.1.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-until-or-while-binding-is-value">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <while|until> <name> is[ not] "<value>"
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while an element or attribute is equal to a value (or not) using a 1 second delay interval and 1 minute timeout period. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the @Delay and @Timeout annotations.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to repeatedly execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the element or attribute to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> to negate the condition</li>
    <li><code>value</code> is the given value</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
   Given the state code can be located by name "state"
    When I navigate to "https://example.com?state=Victoria"
     And I refresh the current page while the state code is not "VIC"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-until-or-while-binding-is-value">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.1.0">v4.1.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-until-or-while-binding-match">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <while|until> <name> <match> "<expression>"`
  ```
  
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while an element or attribute matches an expression using a 1 second delay interval and 1 minute timeout period. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the @Delay and @Timeout annotations.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to repeatedly execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the element or attribute to check</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>contains</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>starts with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>ends with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>matches regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>matches xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>matches json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>matches template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>matches template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
   Given the state code can be located by name "state"
    When I navigate to "https://example.com?state=${the state code}"
     And I refresh the current page until the state code matches regex "(VIC|NSW)"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-until-or-while-binding-match">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.1.0">v4.1.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-until-or-while-binding-not-match">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> <while|until> <name> does not <match> "<expression>"`
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly exectues a step until or while an element or attribute does not match an expression using a 1 second delay interval and 1 minute timeout period. The default delay and timeout can be overridden using the @Delay and @Timeout annotations.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to repeatedly execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the element or attribute to check</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>matche regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>matche xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>matche json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>matche template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>matche template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
   Given the state code can be located by name "state"
    When I navigate to "https://example.com?state=${the state code}"
     And I refresh the current page until the state code does not match regex "(VIC|NSW)"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-until-or-while-binding-not-match">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v4.1.0">v4.1.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### If

<details id="step-if-condition">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> if[ not] <condition>
  ```
  <p>Executes a step depending on whether or not a JS condition evaluates to true.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to potentially execute</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the condition if included (Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.4.0">v3.4.0</Link>)</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;condition&gt;</code> is either:
      <ul>
        <li>
          Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.54.0">v3.54.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li>the name of any binding that will return <code>true</code> when the condition is satisfied or <code>false</code> when it is not</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
        <li>
          Or in prior versions
          <ul>
            <li>the name of a binding containing a javascript function or expression that will return <code>true</code> when the condition is satisfied or <code>false</code> when it is not</li>
            <li>the name of a binding containing a <code>true</code> or <code>false</code> value literal, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.50.0">v3.50.0</Link></li>
          </ul>
        </li>
        <li>Since v3.14.1, the condition name cannot contain double qutoes</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {12,13}
    Given the search field can be located by name "q"
      And topic is "Automation Bindings"
      And topic link can be located by partial link text "${topic}"
      And topic found is defined by js
          """
          [...document.querySelectorAll("a")]
              .filter(a => a.textContent.includes('${topic}'))
              .length > 0
          """
     When I navigate to "https://google.com"
      And I enter "automation" in the search field
      And I click topic link if topic found
     Then the page title should contain "${topic}" if topic found
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-if-condition">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-if-element-condition">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> if <element> is[ not] <state>
  ```
  <p>Executes a step depending on whether or not an element is in a given state.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to potentially execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to check the state of</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the state if included</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;state&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>displayed</code> to execute the step if the element is displayed</li>
        <li><code>hidden</code> to execute the step if the element is not displayed</li>
        <li><code>checked</code> or <code>ticked</code> to execute the step if a checkbox is ticked</li>
        <li><code>unchecked</code> or <code>unticked</code> to execute the step if a checkbox is not ticked</li>
        <li><code>enabled</code> to execute the step if the element is enabled</li>
        <li><code>disabled</code> to execute the step if the element is disabled</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {6}
    Given the search field can be located by name "q"
      And topic is "Automation"
      And topic link can be located by partial link text "${topic}"
     When I navigate to "https://google.com"
      And I enter "automation" in the search field
      And I click topic link if topic link is displayed
     Then the page title should contain "${topic}"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-if-element-condition">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.33.0">v3.33.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-if-binding-defined">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> if <name> is[ not] defined
  ```
  <p>Executes a step depending on whether or not an attribute is bound in the global or current scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to potentially execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the attribute to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> include to execute step if attribute is not bound</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  Given the CSV file: lookup/StateCodes.csv

  ```csv {3}
  Code,Name
  ACT,Australian Capital Territory
  NSW,New South Wales
  NT,Northern Territory
  QLD,Queensland
  SA,South Australia
  TAS,Tasmania
  VIC,Victoria
  WA,Western Australia
  ```

  The following will bind "New South Wales" in the 2nd record to <code>state name</code> in the global scope
  ```gherkin {3}
   Given the state code is "UNKNOWN"
    When I lookup Name in the "lookup/StateCodes.csv" file as state name where "'${data.record.Code}' == '${the state code}'"
    Then unresolved is "true" if state name is not defined
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-if-binding-defined">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.33.0">v3.33.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-if-binding-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> if <name> is[ not] <blank|empty>
  ```
  <p>Executes a step depending on whether or not an element or attribute is bound to a blank or empty value.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to potentially execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the element or attribute to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> include to execute step if attribute is not blank</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2-3}
   Given the state code can be located by name "state"
    When I navigate to "https://example.com" if the state code is blank
     And I navigate to "https://example.com?state=${the state code}" if the state code is not blank
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-if-binding-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.59.0">v3.59.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-if-binding-is-value">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> if <name> is[ not] "<value>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a step depending on whether or not an element or attribute is equal to a value.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to potentially execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the element or attribute to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> include to execute step if the attribute is not equal to the given value</li>
    <li><code>value</code> is the given value</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2-3}
   Given the state code can be located by name "state"
    When I navigate to "https://example.com?state=Victoria" if the state code is "VIC"
     And I navigate to "https://example.com?state=Other" if the state code is not "VIC"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-if-binding-is-value">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.59.0">v3.59.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-if-binding-match">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> if <name> <match> "<expression>"`
  ```
  <p>Executes a step depending on whether or not an element or attribute matches an expression.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to potentially execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the element or attribute to check</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>contains</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>starts with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>ends with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>matches regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>matches xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>matches json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>matches template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>matches template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
   Given the state code can be located by name "state"
    When I navigate to "https://example.com?state=${the state code}" if the state code matches regex "(VIC|NSW)"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-if-binding-match">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.59.0">v3.59.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-if-binding-not-match">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> if <name> does not <match> "<expression>"`
  ```
  <p>Executes a step depending on whether or not an element or attribute does not match an expression.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to potentially execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the element or attribute to check</li>
    <li>
      <code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>matche regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>matche xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>matche json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>matche template</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>matche template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
   Given the state code can be located by name "state"
    When I navigate to "https://example.com?state=${the state code}" if the state code does not match regex "(QLD|NT|wA)"
  ```

  Trimming and ignoring case (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.62.0">v3.62.0</Link>)
  <ul>
    <li>The <code>@Trim</code> annotation can be used on step to trim strings when comparing</li>
    <li>The <code>@IgnoreCase</code> annotation can be used on step to ignore case when comparing</li>
  </ul>

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-if-binding-not-match">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.59.0">v3.59.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-if-filepath-exists">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> if "<filepath>" file[ not] exists
  ```
  <p>Executes a step if a file exists (or not).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to potentially execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file</li>
    <li><code>not</code> to execute step if file does not exist (negation)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin
     Then call step 1 if "path/to/filename1.csv" file exists
      And call step 2 if "path/to/filename2.csv" file not exists
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-if-filepath-exists">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-if-filepath-does-not-exist">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> if "<filepath>" file does not exist
  ```
  <p>Executes a step if a file does not exist.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to potentially execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin
      And call step 2 if "path/to/filename2.csv" file does not exist
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-if-filepath-does-not-exist">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="step-if-filepathref-exists">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <step> if <filepathRef file>[ not] exists
  ```
  <p>Executes a step if a file exists (or not).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to potentially execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file</li>
    <li><code>not</code> to execute step if file does not exist (negation)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {2-3}
    Given my file is "path/to/filename.csv"
     Then call step 1 if my file exists
      And call step 2 if my file not exists
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#step-if-filepathref-exists">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.75.0">v3.75.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

  ```gherkin
  <step> if <filepathRef file> does not exist
  ```
  <p>Executes a step if a file does not exist.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;step&gt;</code> is the DSL step or StepDef to potentially execute</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef file&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
      And call step 2 if my file does not exist
  ```
